# loop over OIA variables
# print incremental sections

for (i_var in buffer_variables_addition) {
  # i_var <- buffer_variables_addition[3]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_buffer_addition_depth_layer <-
    buffer_addition_depth_layer %>%
    filter(variable == i_var) %>%
    select(lon, lat, depth, tref, sensitivity)
  
  # set endpoints and breaks of color scale

  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks_buffer_variables_addition(i_var)
  i_breaks        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_contour_level <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[2])
  i_legend_title  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])
  
  p_maps <-
    i_buffer_addition_depth_layer %>%
    filter(tref == 2014) %>% 
    mutate(tref = paste0("1800-", tref)) %>% 
    p_map_mdim_robinson(
      dim_row = "depth",
      dim_col = "tref",
      var = "sensitivity",
      # contour_level = i_contour_level,
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      breaks = i_breaks,
      col_scale = "cividis",
      n_labels = 2,
      legend_position = "top"
    ) &
    theme(strip.text = element_blank())
  
  breaks_test <- i_breaks[!i_breaks == Inf]
  breaks_test <- breaks_test[!breaks_test == -Inf]
  breaks_reverse <-
    abs(first(breaks_test)) < abs(last(breaks_test))
  
  p_zonal <-
    buffer_addition_depth_layer_zonal %>%
    filter(variable == i_var) %>%
    mutate(depth = str_split(depth, ": ", simplify = TRUE)[, 2]) %>%
    mutate(depth = fct_inorder(depth)) %>% 
    ggplot() +
    geom_ribbon(aes(x = sensitivity, 
                    xmin = sensitivity - sensitivity_sd,
                    xmax = sensitivity + sensitivity_sd,
                    y = lat, 
                    fill = tref),
                alpha = 0.3) +
    geom_path(aes(sensitivity, lat, col = tref, linewidth = tref)) +
    scale_y_continuous(breaks = seq(-45,45,45),
                       position = "right",
                       labels = c("45°N", "Eq.", "45°S")) +
    scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(0.5,rep(1,3))) +
    scale_color_manual(values = four_year_colors) +
    scale_fill_manual(values = four_year_colors) +
    guides(
      fill = guide_legend(ncol = 2),
      col = guide_legend(ncol = 2)
    ) +
    labs(x = i_legend_title,
         y = "Latitude (°N)",
         title = "Zonal means") +
    coord_cartesian(expand = 0) +
    theme_classic() +
    theme(axis.title.x = element_markdown(),
          axis.text.y = element_text(hjust = 1),
          axis.title.y = element_blank(),
          strip.text = element_text(size = 14),
          strip.background = element_blank(),
          legend.position = "top",
          legend.title = element_blank(),
          legend.direction = "vertical"
          ) +
    facet_grid(depth ~.,
               switch = "y")
  
  if (breaks_reverse == TRUE) {
    p_zonal <- p_zonal +
          scale_x_continuous(breaks = as.numeric(i_breaks)[c(FALSE, TRUE)])
    
  } else{
    p_zonal <- p_zonal +
          scale_x_reverse(breaks = as.numeric(i_breaks)[c(FALSE, TRUE)])
  }
    
  p_trends <-
  buffer_addition_depth_layer_trend %>%
    filter(variable == i_var) %>%
    ggplot() +
    geom_ribbon(
      aes(
        x = pCO2,
        ymin = sensitivity - sensitivity_sd,
        ymax = sensitivity + sensitivity_sd,
        fill = biome,
        group = biome
      ),
      alpha = 0.3
    ) +
    geom_path(aes(
      pCO2, sensitivity,
      col = biome, group = biome, linewidth = biome
    )) +
    geom_point(
      aes(
        pCO2, sensitivity,
        col = biome, group = biome, size = biome
      ),
      shape = 21, fill = "white"
    ) +
    geom_path(data = . %>% filter(biome == "Global"),
              aes(
      pCO2, sensitivity,
      col = biome, group = biome, linewidth = biome
    )) +
    geom_point(data = . %>% filter(biome == "Global"),
      aes(
        pCO2, sensitivity,
        col = biome, group = biome, size = biome
      ),
      shape = 21, fill = "white"
    ) +
    scale_x_continuous(breaks = seq(280, 400, 40)) +
    scale_color_manual(values = biome_colors) +
    scale_fill_manual(values = biome_colors) +
    scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(1, rep(0.5, 5))) +
    scale_size_manual(values = c(1.5, rep(0, 5))) +
    guides(
      fill = guide_legend(ncol = 2),
      col = guide_legend(ncol = 2),
      size = guide_legend(ncol = 2),
      linewidth = guide_legend(ncol = 2)
    ) +
    labs(
      y = str_replace(i_legend_title, "<br>", " "),
      x = expression(pCO["2,atm"] ~ (ppm)),
      title = "Biome means"
    ) +
    theme_classic() +
    theme(
      axis.title.y.right = element_markdown(),
      strip.background = element_blank(),
      strip.text = element_blank(),
      legend.title = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "top",
      legend.direction = "vertical"
    ) +
    facet_grid(depth ~ .)
  
  if (breaks_reverse == TRUE) {
    p_trends <- p_trends +
          scale_y_continuous(breaks = as.numeric(i_breaks)[c(FALSE, TRUE)],
                             position = "right")
    
  } else{
    p_trends <- p_trends +
          scale_y_reverse(breaks = as.numeric(i_breaks)[c(FALSE, TRUE)],
                             position = "right")
  }
  
  
  p_zonal + p_maps + p_trends +
    plot_layout(widths = c(1,4,1.5))
  

  ggsave(
    here::here(
      paste0(
        "output/supplement/maps_depth_layer_",
        i_var,
        "_buffer_additional.png"
      )
    ),
    width = 10,
    height = 10,
    dpi = 600,
    bg = "white"
  )
  
}

buffer_addition_depth_layer_relative <-
  buffer_addition_depth_layer %>%
  filter(variable %in% OIA_variables[-1]) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = sensitivity) %>%
  mutate(`1900` = (`1800` + `1994`) / 2,
         delta_sensitivity = abs(100 * (`2004` - `1900`) / `1900`)) %>%
  select(lon, lat, depth, variable, delta_sensitivity)

i_breaks        <- c(-Inf, seq(0, 24, 4), Inf)
i_legend_title  <- "Sensitivity 2004<br>(% of ~1900)"

    dim_col = "variable",
    var = "delta_sensitivity",

    breaks = i_breaks,

for (i_var in buffer_variables_addition) {
  # i_var <- buffer_variables_addition[4]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_buffer_addition_depth_layer_relative <-
    buffer_addition_depth_layer_relative %>%
    filter(variable == i_var) %>%
    select(lon, lat, depth, delta_sensitivity)
  
  # determine endpoints and breaks of color scale
  
  low <- i_buffer_addition_depth_layer_relative %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_sensitivity)) %>%
    pull(delta_sensitivity) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_low), names = FALSE)

  high <- i_buffer_addition_depth_layer_relative %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_sensitivity)) %>%
    pull(delta_sensitivity) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_high), names = FALSE)

  i_breaks <- signif(c(-Inf, seq(low, high, length.out = break_numbers), Inf),2)
  
  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks_buffer_variables_addition_change(i_var)
  i_breaks        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_contour_level <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[2])
  i_legend_title  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])
  
  i_buffer_addition_depth_layer_relative %>%
    p_map_mdim_robinson(
      dim_row = "depth",
      var = "delta_sensitivity",
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      breaks = i_breaks,
      legend_position = "right"
    )
  
  ggsave(
    here::here(
      paste0(
        "output/all_variables/maps_depth_layer_",
        i_var,
        "_buffer_additional_change_relative_to_absolute.png"
      )
    ),
    width = 6,
    height = 5,
    dpi = 600,
    bg = "white"
  )

for (i_var in buffer_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[1]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_buffer_climatology_depth_layer <-
    buffer_climatology_depth_layer %>%
    filter(variable == i_var) %>%
    select(lon, lat, depth, tref, value)
  
  # determine endpoints and breaks of color scale
  
  low <- i_buffer_climatology_depth_layer %>%
    filter(!is.na(value)) %>%
    pull(value) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_low), names = FALSE)
  
  high <- i_buffer_climatology_depth_layer %>%
    filter(!is.na(value)) %>%
    pull(value) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_high), names = FALSE)
  
  breaks <- c(-Inf, seq(low, high, length.out = break_numbers), Inf)
  
  p_climatology <-
    i_buffer_climatology_depth_layer %>%
    p_map_mdim_robinson(
      dim_row = "depth",
      dim_col = "tref",
      var = "value",
      legend_title = i_var,
      breaks = breaks,
      legend_position = "right"
    )
  
  print(p_climatology)
  
}

dev.off()

rm(buffer_climatology_depth_layer,
   i_buffer_climatology_depth_layer)

CO2 System speciation

biome_co2_speciation <-
  inner_join(
    biomemask,
    acidification_depth_layer %>%
      select(lon, lat, depth, tref,
             talk, tco2, temp, sal, phosphate, silicate)
  ) %>%
  select(-c(lon, lat)) %>%
  group_by(biome, depth, tref) %>%
  summarise(across(where(is.numeric), ~ wmean(x = ., weights = area))) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  select(-area) %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref))


biome_co2_speciation <-
  biome_co2_speciation %>%
  mutate(
    depth_calc = case_when(
      depth == "A: 0 - 100 m"     ~ 50,
      depth == "B: 100 - 500 m"   ~ 300,
      depth == "C: 500 - 1500 m"  ~ 1000,
      depth == "D: 1500 - 3000 m" ~ 2250
    )
  ) 


biome_co2_speciation_abs <-
  biome_co2_speciation %>%
  mutate(
    sir(
      flag = 15,
      var1 = talk * 1e-6,
      var2 = tco2 * 1e-6,
      S = sal,
      T = temp,
      P = depth_calc / 10,
      Pt = phosphate * 1e-6,
      Sit = silicate * 1e-6,
      k1k2 = "s20",
      kf = "dg",
      pHscale = "T"
    )[c(7,14,15,18,21)]
  )

biome_co2_speciation_delta <-
  biome_co2_speciation_abs %>%
  rename(H_free_abs = H_free,
         OmegaAragonite_abs = OmegaAragonite,
         CO2_abs = CO2,
         CO3_abs = CO3,
         HCO3_abs = HCO3) %>%
  mutate(
    sir(
      flag = 15,
      var1 = talk * 1e-6,
      var2 = (tco2 + 1) * 1e-6,
      S = sal,
      T = temp,
      P = depth_calc / 10,
      Pt = phosphate * 1e-6,
      Sit = silicate * 1e-6,
      k1k2 = "s20",
      kf = "dg",
      pHscale = "T"
    )[c(7,14,15,18,21)]
  ) %>%
  mutate(H_free = H_free - H_free_abs,
         OmegaAragonite = OmegaAragonite - OmegaAragonite_abs,
         CO2 = CO2 - CO2_abs,
         CO3 = CO3 - CO3_abs,
         HCO3 = HCO3 - HCO3_abs) %>%
  select(-contains("_abs"))


biome_co2_speciation <-
  bind_rows(
    biome_co2_speciation_abs %>% mutate(estimate = "absolute"),
    biome_co2_speciation_delta %>% mutate(estimate = "sensitivity")
  ) %>%
  select(biome, depth, tref, CO2:estimate)


biome_co2_speciation %>% 
  filter(estimate == "sensitivity") %>% 
  group_by(biome, depth, tref) %>% 
  summarise(delta_tco2 = (CO2 + HCO3 + CO3)*1e6) %>% 
  ungroup()

  pivot_longer(H_free:OmegaAragonite) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = estimate,
              values_from = value) %>%

  mutate(depth = fct_inorder(depth)) 


for(i_var in OIA_variables_core){

  # i_var <- OIA_variables_core[1]
  
    
  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks_buffer_variables_addition(i_var)
  i_breaks        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_legend_title  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])
    
  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks_absolute(i_var)
  i_breaks_abs        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_legend_title_abs  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])
  
  p_speciation <- 
  biome_co2_speciation %>%
    filter(name == i_var) %>% 
    ggplot(aes(
      absolute,
      sensitivity,
      fill = depth,
      shape = biome,
      alpha = tref,
      group = interaction(biome, depth)
    )) +
    geom_path() +
    geom_point() +
    scale_fill_viridis_d(option = "mako",
                         direction = -1) +
    scale_alpha_discrete(range = c(0.4, 1)) +
    scale_shape_manual(values = 21:25) +
    guides(fill = guide_legend(override.aes = list(shape = 21),
                               order = 1)) +
    # scale_x_continuous(breaks = unname(i_breaks_abs)) +
    # scale_y_continuous(breaks = unname(i_breaks)) +
    labs(x = i_legend_title_abs,
         y = i_legend_title) +
    guides(shape = guide_legend(byrow = TRUE)) +
    theme(
      legend.spacing.y = unit(0.2, 'cm'),
      legend.title = element_blank(),
      axis.title.x = element_markdown(),
      axis.title.y = element_markdown(),
      aspect.ratio = 1
    )
  
    
  if (i_var == "H_free") {
    p_speciation_H_free <- p_speciation
  }
    
  if (i_var == "OmegaAragonite") {
    p_speciation_OmegaAragonite <- p_speciation
  }

}

acidification_bottom_area <-
  acidification_bottom_area %>%
  mutate(area = earth_surf(lat, lon))

acidification_bottom_raw <-
  left_join(
    acidification_bottom_area %>%
      select(lon, lat, depth, area),
    acidification_volume_raw
  )


bottom_area_total <-
  acidification_bottom_area %>%
  summarise(area_total = sum(area)) %>%
  pull()

acidification_volume_raw <-
  acidification_volume_raw %>%
  pivot_longer(all_of(OIA_variables),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total")

acidification_bottom_raw <-
  acidification_bottom_raw %>%
  pivot_longer(all_of(OIA_variables),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total")
gc()

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[4]
  
  i_contours <- labels_breaks(i_var)$i_breaks
  
  # determine volume changes
  
  i_acidification_volume_raw <- acidification_volume_raw %>%
    filter(variable == i_var)
  
  acidification_volume_binned <-
    left_join(i_acidification_volume_raw,
              ocean_volume_mask) %>%
    mutate(delta_total = cut(delta_total, i_contours)) %>%
    group_by(tref,
             delta_total,
             variable,
             MLR_basin_mask,
             MLR_configuration) %>%
    summarise(volume = sum(volume_total, na.rm = TRUE)) %>%
    ungroup()
  
  i_acidification_bottom_raw <- acidification_bottom_raw %>%
    filter(variable == i_var)
  
  acidification_bottom_binned <-
    i_acidification_bottom_raw %>%
    mutate(delta_total = cut(delta_total, i_contours)) %>%
    group_by(tref, variable, delta_total,
             MLR_basin_mask,
             MLR_configuration) %>%
    summarise(area = sum(area, na.rm = TRUE)) %>%
    ungroup()
  
  acidification_volume_binned <-
    full_join(acidification_bottom_binned,
              acidification_volume_binned)
  
  
  if (exists("acidification_volume_binned_all")) {
    acidification_volume_binned_all <-
      bind_rows(acidification_volume_binned_all,
                acidification_volume_binned)
  }

  if (!exists("acidification_volume_binned_all")) {
    acidification_volume_binned_all <-
      acidification_volume_binned
  }
  
  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks(i_var)
  i_breaks        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_contour_level <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[2])
  i_legend_title  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])
  
  p_map <-
    i_acidification_bottom_raw %>%
    filter(
      tref == "2014",
      MLR_basin_mask == MLR_basin_mask_reference,
      MLR_configuration == MLR_configuration_reference
    ) %>%
    select(lon, lat, delta_total) %>%
    p_map_mdim_robinson(
      var = "delta_total",
      col_scale = "RdPu",
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      breaks = i_breaks,
      n_labels = 2,
      legend_position = "top"
    ) &
    theme(strip.text = element_blank())
  
  if (i_var == "tco2") {
    p_map_tco2 <- p_map
  }
  
  if (i_var == "H_free") {
    p_map_H_free <- p_map
  }
  
  if (i_var == "OmegaAragonite") {
    p_map_OmegaAragonite <- p_map
  }
  
}

rm(acidification_volume_binned,
   acidification_bottom_binned)

                 p_map_H_free,
                 p_map_tco2,
                 ncol = 1))

      rename_at(c("area", "volume"),
                ~ paste0(.x, "_interval_mean")) %>% 
      rename(name = variable),
    mode = "delta_total")[[1]]

acidification_volume_binned_all <-
  acidification_volume_binned_all %>%
  mutate(
    across(std_case, ~replace_na(.x, 0))
  )

volume_total <-
  ocean_volume_integration_depth %>%
  filter(depth_integration == depth_integration_acidification) %>%
  pull(volume_total)

acidification_volume_binned_all <-
  full_join(acidification_volume_binned_all,
            tibble(
              total = c(volume_total, bottom_area_total),
              variable = c("volume", "area")
            ))

acidification_volume_binned_all <-
  acidification_volume_binned_all %>%
  mutate(
    tref = as.factor(tref),
    delta_total = fct_relevel(delta_total, "(0, Inf]", after = Inf),
    std_case = 100 * std_case / total,
    sd = 100 * sd / total
  )


y_max_vol <- acidification_volume_binned_all %>%
  filter(
    name %in% c("OmegaAragonite",
                    "H_free",
                    "tco2")
  ) %>%
  summarise(max(std_case + sd)) %>%
  pull() * 1.05


acidification_volume_binned_all <-
acidification_volume_binned_all %>%
  mutate(
    delta_total_num = case_when(
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-Inf,-0.8]" ~ -0.9,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.8,-0.7]" ~ -0.8,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.7,-0.6]" ~ -0.7,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.6,-0.5]" ~ -0.6,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.5,-0.4]" ~ -0.5,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.4,-0.3]" ~ -0.4,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.3,-0.2]" ~ -0.3,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.2,-0.1]" ~ -0.2,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(-0.1,0]"    ~ -0.1,
      name == "OmegaAragonite" & delta_total == "(0, Inf]"    ~ -0.0,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(-Inf,0]"   ~ -0.4,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(0,0.4]"    ~ 0,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(0.4,0.8]"  ~ 0.4,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(0.8,1.2]"  ~ 0.8,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(1.2,1.6]"  ~ 1.2,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(1.6,2]"    ~ 1.6,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(2,2.4]"    ~ 2,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(2.4,2.8]"  ~ 2.4,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(2.8,3.2]"  ~ 2.8,
      name == "H_free" & delta_total ==  "(3.2, Inf]" ~ 3.2,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(-Inf,0]" ~ -10,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(0,10]"   ~ 0,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(10,20]"  ~ 10,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(20,30]"  ~ 20,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(30,40]"  ~ 30,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(40,50]"  ~ 40,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(50,60]"  ~ 50,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(60,70]"  ~ 60,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(70,80]"  ~ 70,
      name == "tco2" & delta_total == "(80, Inf]"~ 80
    ),
    delta_total_max = case_when(
      name == "OmegaAragonite" ~ -0.5,
      name == "H_free" ~ 1.999,
      name == "tco2" ~ 49.99,
    )
  ) %>% 
  filter(!is.na(delta_total_num))

acidification_volume_binned_all_peak_sum <-
  acidification_volume_binned_all %>%
  filter(
    abs(delta_total_num) > abs(delta_total_max)
  ) %>%
  group_by(variable, name, tref, delta_total_max) %>%
  summarise(std_case = sum(std_case),
            sd = sqrt(sum(sd^2))) %>%
  ungroup()

acidification_volume_binned_all_peak_sum <-
  acidification_volume_binned_all_peak_sum %>%
  mutate(
    tref = as.numeric(as.character(tref)),
    x_pos = delta_total_max * 1.4,
    y_pos = y_max_vol * 0.8 + (tref - 2004) / 2,
    label_text = paste(round(std_case), "±", round(sd), "%")
  )

p_vol_OmegaAragonite <-
  acidification_volume_binned_all %>%
  filter(name == "OmegaAragonite",
         variable == "volume") %>%
  ggplot() +
  geom_vline(aes(xintercept = delta_total_max)) +
  geom_rect(
    data = . %>% filter(delta_total_num != 0),
    aes(
      xmax = delta_total_num + 0.1,
      xmin = delta_total_num,
      ymax = std_case + sd,
      ymin = std_case - sd,
      fill = tref
    ),
    alpha = 0.3
  ) +
  geom_text(
    data = acidification_volume_binned_all_peak_sum %>%
      filter(name == "OmegaAragonite",
         variable == "volume"),
    aes(
      x = x_pos,
      y = y_pos,
      label = label_text,
      col = as.factor(tref)
    ),
    show.legend = FALSE
  ) +
  geom_step(
    aes(delta_total_num,
        std_case,
        col = tref),
    direction = "vh",
    linewidth = 1
  ) +
  scale_color_manual(values = three_year_colors, name = "Change from\n1800 to:") +
  scale_fill_manual(values = three_year_colors, name = "Change from\n1800 to:") +
  scale_x_reverse(breaks = -seq(0, 0.8, 0.2)) +
  scale_y_continuous(limits = c(0, y_max_vol)) +
  coord_cartesian(expand = 0) +
  facet_wrap( ~ name,
              scales = "free_x",
              labeller = labeller(name = x_axis_labels)) +
  theme(
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_markdown(),
    legend.position = "top",
    legend.title.align = 1,
    axis.title = element_blank()
  )

      y = y_pos,
      label = label_text,
      col = as.factor(tref)
    ),
    show.legend = FALSE
  ) +
  geom_step(
    aes(delta_total_num + 0.4,
        std_case,
        col = tref),
    direction = "vh",
    linewidth = 1
  ) +
  scale_color_manual(values = three_year_colors, name = "1800 - ") +
  scale_fill_manual(values = three_year_colors, name = "1800 - ") +
  scale_x_continuous(breaks = seq(0, 3.2, 0.8),
                     limits = c(0, NA)) +
  scale_y_continuous(limits = c(0, y_max_vol)) +
  coord_cartesian(expand = 0) +
  facet_wrap( ~ name,
              scales = "free_x",
              labeller = labeller(name = x_axis_labels)) +
  labs(y = paste0(
    "Acidified volume (% of top ",
    depth_integration_acidification,
    "m)"
  )) +
  theme(
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_markdown(),
    legend.position = "none",
    axis.title.x = element_blank()
  )

Saturation state changes

Horizon maps

acidification_saturation_horizon <- acidification_trend %>%
  select(lat, lon, depth, tref,
         contains("Omega"),
         -contains("delta"))

acidification_saturation_horizon <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon %>%
  pivot_longer(
    contains("Omega"),
    names_to = "mineral",
    names_prefix = "Omega",
    values_to = "Omega"
  )

acidification_saturation_horizon %>%
  group_by(tref, mineral) %>%
  summarise(n()) %>%
  ungroup()
# A tibble: 8 × 3
   tref mineral    `n()`
  <dbl> <chr>      <int>
1  1800 Aragonite 943832
2  1800 Calcite   943832
3  1994 Aragonite 943832
4  1994 Calcite   943832
5  2004 Aragonite 943832
6  2004 Calcite   943832
7  2014 Aragonite 943832
8  2014 Calcite   943832
bathymetry <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon %>%
  group_by(lat, lon, tref, mineral) %>%
  summarise(depth = max(depth)) %>%
  ungroup()

# bathymetry %>% 
#   ggplot(aes(lon, lat, fill = depth)) +
#   geom_tile() +
#   scale_fill_viridis_c(direction = -1) +
#   coord_quickmap() +
#   facet_grid(mineral ~ tref)

for(i_sat_level in c(5, 4, 3.5, 3, 2, 1.5, 1)) {
  
  # i_sat_level <- 2
  
  
  # filter undersaturated water masses
  
  undersaturated <- 
    acidification_saturation_horizon %>%
    filter(Omega < i_sat_level)
  
  
  # detect shallowest depth below exact saturation horizon
  
  saturation_horizon_deep <-
    undersaturated %>%
    group_by(lat, lon, tref, mineral) %>%
    mutate(saturation_horizon_deep = min(depth)) %>%
    ungroup() %>% 
    filter(depth == saturation_horizon_deep)
  
  # detect shallowest depth above exact saturation horizon
  
  saturation_horizon_shallow <-
    inner_join(
      acidification_saturation_horizon,
      saturation_horizon_deep %>%
        select(lat, lon, tref, mineral,
               saturation_horizon_deep)
    )
  
  saturation_horizon_shallow <-
    saturation_horizon_shallow %>%
    filter(depth < saturation_horizon_deep) %>%
    group_by(lat, lon, tref, mineral) %>%
    mutate(saturation_horizon_shallow = max(depth)) %>%
    ungroup() %>% 
    filter(depth == saturation_horizon_shallow)
  
  # join depth horizons above and below shallowest saturation horizon
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    bind_rows(saturation_horizon_deep,
              saturation_horizon_shallow) %>%
    select(-contains("saturation_horizon"))
  
  # interpolate to exact saturation horizon depth
  
  surface_grid <- saturation_horizon %>% 
    distinct(lat, lon, tref, mineral)
  
  surface_grid <-
    expand_grid(
      surface_grid,
      Omega = i_sat_level
    )
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    full_join(saturation_horizon,
              surface_grid)
  
  rm(surface_grid)
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    saturation_horizon %>%
    group_by(lon, lat, tref, mineral) %>%
    mutate(n = n()) %>%
    ungroup()
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    saturation_horizon %>%
    filter(n == 3) %>%
    select(-n)
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    saturation_horizon %>%
    arrange(lat, lon, tref, mineral, Omega) %>% 
    group_by(lon, lat, tref, mineral) %>%
    mutate(depth = approxfun(Omega, depth, rule = 1)(Omega)) %>%
    ungroup()
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    saturation_horizon %>%
    filter(Omega == i_sat_level) %>%
    select(lon, lat, tref, mineral, depth)
  
  print(
    nrow(saturation_horizon) == nrow(saturation_horizon_shallow))
  
  # fill regions with saturation horizon at surface
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    bind_rows(
      saturation_horizon,
      saturation_horizon_deep %>%
        filter(saturation_horizon_deep == 0) %>%
        select(lon, lat, tref, depth, mineral, depth)
    )
  
  # fill other regions with bathymetry
  
  bathymetry_fill <-
    anti_join(bathymetry,
              saturation_horizon %>%
                select(lat, lon, tref, mineral))
  
  saturation_horizon <-
    bind_rows(
      saturation_horizon,
      bathymetry_fill
    )
  
  saturation_horizon <- saturation_horizon %>%
    mutate(sat_level = i_sat_level)
  
  
  rm(saturation_horizon_deep,
     saturation_horizon_shallow,
     bathymetry_fill)
  
  if (exists("acidification_saturation_horizon_levels")) {
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels <-
      bind_rows(acidification_saturation_horizon_levels,
                saturation_horizon)
  }
  
  if (!exists("acidification_saturation_horizon_levels")) {
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels <- saturation_horizon
  }
  
}

saturation_horizon_outlier <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels %>%
  filter(depth >= 1000 &
           mineral == "Aragonite" &
           sat_level >= 3.5) %>%
  distinct(lat, lon, sat_level,
           mineral)

p_sat_absolute <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels %>%
  relocate(lon) %>%
  filter(tref == 2014,
         mineral == "Aragonite",
         sat_level %in% c(1,3,4),
         depth != 0) %>%
  select(-c(tref, mineral)) %>%
  p_map_mdim_robinson(
    dim_row = "sat_level",
    var = "depth",
    # contour_level = 10,
    # contour_col = "grey20",
    legend_title = paste0("Depth of<br>isosurface<br>2014<br>(m)"),
    legend_position = "left",
    col_scale = "mako",
    breaks = seq(0, 3000, 200)
  )
  

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels %>%
  filter(mineral == "Aragonite") %>%
  select(-c(mineral)) %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(lat, lon, sat_level) %>%
  mutate(
    delta_depth = depth - first(depth),
    delta_depth = if_else(delta_depth == 0,
                          NA,
                          delta_depth),
    period = paste0(first(tref), "-", tref)
  ) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  filter(tref != 1800) %>%
  drop_na() %>%
  select(lon, lat, tref, period, sat_level, delta_depth) 


acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_1994 <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels %>%
  filter(mineral == "Aragonite",
         tref != 1800) %>%
  select(-c(mineral)) %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(lat, lon, sat_level) %>%
  mutate(
    delta_depth = depth - first(depth),
    delta_depth = if_else(delta_depth == 0,
                          NA,
                          delta_depth),
    period = paste0(first(tref), "-", tref)
  ) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  filter(tref != 1994) %>%
  drop_na() %>%
  select(lon, lat, tref, period, sat_level, delta_depth) 



p_sat_change <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change %>%
  filter(sat_level %in% c(1,3,4),
         tref == 2014) %>% 
  select(-tref) %>% 
  mutate(delta_depth = -delta_depth) %>% 
  select(-period) %>% 
  p_map_mdim_robinson(
    dim_row = "sat_level",
    # dim_col = "mineral",
    col_scale = "Rocket",
    var = "delta_depth",
    legend_title = paste0("Shoaling of<br>isosurface<br>1800-2014<br>(m)"),
    legend_position = "right",
    breaks = c(-Inf, seq(0, 300, 50), Inf)
  ) &
  theme(strip.text = element_blank())

# filter existing horizons and join with biome masks

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw <-
  inner_join(
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels %>%
      filter(mineral == "Aragonite",
             depth != 0),
    biomemask
  )

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw <-
  bind_rows(
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw,
    inner_join(
      acidification_saturation_horizon_levels %>%
        relocate(lon) %>%
        filter(mineral == "Aragonite",
               depth != 0),
      biomemask %>%
        mutate(biome = "Global")
    )
  )


acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw %>%
  select(-mineral)

# join atmospheric CO2

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw <-
  right_join(co2_atm_reccap2 %>% rename(tref = year),
             acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw)


acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw %>%
  filter(biome %in% c("Global",
                      "Southern\nOcean"),
         sat_level %in% c(1,3,4)) %>% 
  mutate(depth = cut(
    depth,
    c(0, 100, 500, 1500, 3000),
    c("A: 0 - 100 m", "B: 100 - 500 m", "C: 500 - 1500 m", "D: 1500 - 3000 m"),
    include.lowest = TRUE
  )) %>% 
  group_by(tref, pCO2, biome, sat_level, depth) %>% 
  summarise(area = sum(area)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  group_by(tref, pCO2, biome, sat_level) %>% 
  mutate(area_fraction = 100 * area / sum(area)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  ggplot(aes(pCO2, area_fraction)) +
  geom_path(aes(col = depth)) +
  geom_point(aes(fill = depth, shape = depth)) +
  scale_color_viridis_d(option = "mako", direction = -1) +
  scale_fill_viridis_d(option = "mako", direction = -1) +
  scale_shape_manual(values = 21:24) +
  facet_grid(sat_level ~ biome)

# Horizon medians and quantiles

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome <-
  acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome_raw %>%
  group_by(biome, tref, pCO2, sat_level) %>%
  summarise(
    depth_01 = quantile(depth, 0.1, na.rm = TRUE),
    depth_025 = quantile(depth, 0.25, na.rm = TRUE),
    depth_sd = wsd(depth, area),
    depth = wmean(depth, area),
    grid_cells = n()
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

# Changes in saturation horizon by biome

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_biome <-
  inner_join(acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change,
             biomemask) %>%
  group_by(biome, period, tref, sat_level) %>%
  summarise(
    delta_depth_01 = quantile(delta_depth, 0.1, na.rm = TRUE),
    delta_depth_025 = quantile(delta_depth, 0.25, na.rm = TRUE),
    delta_depth_sd = wsd(delta_depth, area),
    delta_depth = wmean(delta_depth, area),
    delta_grid_cells = n()
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_global <-
  inner_join(
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change,
    biomemask %>%
      mutate(biome = "Global")
  ) %>%
  group_by(biome, period, tref, sat_level) %>%
  summarise(
    delta_depth_01 = quantile(delta_depth, 0.1, na.rm = TRUE),
    delta_depth_025 = quantile(delta_depth, 0.25, na.rm = TRUE),
    delta_depth_sd = wsd(delta_depth, area),
    delta_depth = wmean(delta_depth, area),
    delta_grid_cells = n()
  ) %>%
  ungroup()



acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_biome <-
  bind_rows(
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_global,
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_biome
  )

rm(acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_global)

4ec0a9f jens-daniel-mueller 2023-11-28

Volume incl uncertainty

acidification_saturation_horizon <-
  acidification_trend_uncertainty_absolute %>%
  select(lat,
         lon,
         depth,
         tref,
         MLR_basin_mask,
         MLR_configuration,
         OmegaAragonite) %>%
  filter(depth <= ocean_depth)


for (i_sat_level in c(5, 4, 3.5, 3, 2, 1.5, 1)) {
  # i_sat_level <- 2
  
  # filter undersaturated water masses
  
  undersaturated <-
    acidification_saturation_horizon %>%
    filter(OmegaAragonite < i_sat_level)
  
  undersaturated_volume <-
    left_join(undersaturated,
              ocean_volume_mask) %>%
    group_by(tref, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
    summarise(volume_undersat = sum(volume_total, na.rm = TRUE)) %>%
    ungroup() %>%
    mutate(sat_level = i_sat_level)
  

  if (exists("undersaturated_volume_all")) {
    undersaturated_volume_all <-
      bind_rows(undersaturated_volume_all,
                undersaturated_volume)
  }
  
  if (!exists("undersaturated_volume_all")) {
    undersaturated_volume_all <- undersaturated_volume
  }
  
  
  saturation_horizon_uncertainty <-
    undersaturated %>%
    group_by(tref, lat, lon, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
    filter(depth == min(depth)) %>%
    ungroup() %>%
    mutate(sat_level = i_sat_level)
  
  
  if (exists("saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all")) {
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all <-
      bind_rows(saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all,
                saturation_horizon_uncertainty)
  }
  
  if (!exists("saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all")) {
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all <- saturation_horizon_uncertainty
  }
  
  
}


# rm(undersaturated_volume_all)

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw <-
  inner_join(
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all %>%
      filter(depth != 0) %>% 
      select(-OmegaAragonite),
    biomemask
  )

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw <-
  bind_rows(
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw,
    inner_join(
      saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all %>%
      filter(depth != 0) %>% 
      select(-OmegaAragonite),
      biomemask %>%
        mutate(biome = "Global")
    )
  )

             saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw)

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_area_fraction <-
saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw %>%
  mutate(depth = cut(
    depth,
    c(0, 100, 500, 1500, 3000),
    c("A: 0 - 100 m", "B: 100 - 500 m", "C: 500 - 1500 m", "D: 1500 - 3000 m"),
    include.lowest = TRUE
  )) %>% 
  group_by(tref, pCO2, biome, sat_level, MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask, depth) %>% 
  summarise(area = sum(area)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  group_by(tref, pCO2, biome, sat_level, MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask) %>% 
  mutate(area_fraction = 100 * area / sum(area)) %>% 
  ungroup() 

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_area_fraction %>% 
  ggplot(aes(pCO2, area_fraction)) +
  geom_path(aes(col = depth, group = interaction(depth, MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask))) +
  geom_point(aes(fill = depth, shape = depth)) +
  scale_color_viridis_d(option = "mako", direction = -1) +
  scale_fill_viridis_d(option = "mako", direction = -1) +
  scale_shape_manual(values = 21:24) +
  facet_grid(sat_level ~ biome)

    df = saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_area_fraction %>%
      rename("area_fraction_interval_mean" = "area_fraction",
             "area_interval_mean" = "area"),
    mode = "delta_total"
  )[[1]]

  saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_area_fraction %>%
  filter(variable == "area_fraction")

# join accurate depth estimate with approximated uncertainty

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome <-
  full_join(
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome %>%
      select(-std_case),
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_biome %>%
      select(-c(depth_sd, grid_cells)) %>%
      pivot_longer(contains("depth"),
                   names_to = "variable",
                   values_to = "std_case")
  )

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome %>%
  drop_na() %>% 
  filter(biome %in% c("Global",
                      "Southern\nOcean"),
         sat_level %in% c(1,3,3.5,4)) %>% 
  mutate(sat_level = as.factor(sat_level)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(
    pCO2,
    std_case,
    ymin = std_case - sd,
    ymax = std_case + sd
  )) +
  geom_ribbon(aes(fill = variable), alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(col = variable)) +
  geom_point(aes(fill = variable), shape = 21, col = "grey20") +
  scale_color_viridis_d() +
  scale_fill_viridis_d() +
  facet_grid(sat_level ~ biome, scales = "free_y")

# determine uncertainty for changes in saturation horizon


saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change <-
  saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw %>%
  group_by(biome, tref, pCO2, sat_level, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  summarise(
    depth_01_interval_mean = quantile(depth, 0.1, na.rm = TRUE),
    depth_025_interval_mean = quantile(depth, 0.25, na.rm = TRUE),
    depth_interval_mean = wmean(depth, area)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()


saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change <-
  bind_rows(
    expand_grid(
      saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change %>%
        filter(tref == 1800,
               MLR_configuration == MLR_configuration_reference) %>%
        select(-c(MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration)),
      saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change %>%
        filter(tref == 1994,
               !str_detect(MLR_configuration, "DIC")) %>%
        distinct(MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration)
    ),
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change
  )
  


saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change %>%
  filter(biome %in% c("Global",
                      "Southern\nOcean"),
         sat_level %in% c(1, 3, 3.5, 4)) %>%
  mutate(sat_level = as.factor(sat_level)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(
    pCO2,
    depth_interval_mean,
    group = interaction(MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask)
  )) +
  geom_path(data = . %>% filter(!str_detect(MLR_configuration, "DIC")),
            aes(col = "CO2 uncertainty")) +
  geom_path(data = . %>% filter(str_detect(MLR_configuration, "DIC")),
            aes(col = "eMLR uncertainty")) +
  facet_grid(sat_level ~ biome, scales = "free_y")

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change_1800  <-
  saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change  %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(biome, sat_level, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  mutate(
    depth_01_interval_mean = depth_01_interval_mean - first(depth_01_interval_mean),
    depth_025_interval_mean = depth_025_interval_mean - first(depth_025_interval_mean),
    depth_interval_mean =  depth_interval_mean - first(depth_interval_mean)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()


saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change_1994  <-
  saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change  %>%
  filter(tref != 1800) %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(biome, sat_level, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  mutate(
    depth_01_interval_mean = depth_01_interval_mean - first(depth_01_interval_mean),
    depth_025_interval_mean = depth_025_interval_mean - first(depth_025_interval_mean),
    depth_interval_mean =  depth_interval_mean - first(depth_interval_mean)
  ) %>%
  ungroup()


table_sat_horizon_rel <-
  saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change_1800 %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("interval_mean")) %>%
  select(-pCO2) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = value,
              values_fn = mean) %>%
  mutate(
    `2014` = 100 * (`2014` - `1994`) / `1994`,
    `2004` = 100 * (`2004` - `1994`) / `1994`,
    `1994` = 0
  ) %>%
  select(-`1800`) %>%
  pivot_longer(c(`1994`, `2004`, `2014`),
               values_to = "value",
               names_to = "tref") %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = name,
              values_from = value)

table_sat_horizon_rel %>%
  ggplot(aes(tref, depth_interval_mean)) +
  geom_point() +
  facet_wrap( ~ biome)

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change <-
  right_join(
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change %>%
      select(-std_case) %>% 
      rename(period = tref),
    acidification_saturation_horizon_levels_change_biome %>%
      select(-c(delta_depth_sd, delta_grid_cells)) %>%
      pivot_longer(contains("depth"),
                   names_to = "variable",
                   values_to = "std_case") %>% 
      mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "delta_"))
  )

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change %>%
  drop_na() %>% 
  filter(biome %in% c("Global",
                      "Southern\nOcean"),
         sat_level %in% c(1,3,3.5,4)) %>% 
  mutate(sat_level = as.factor(sat_level)) %>%
  ggplot(aes(
    pCO2,
    std_case,
    ymin = std_case - sd,
    ymax = std_case + sd
  )) +
  geom_ribbon(aes(fill = variable), alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(col = variable)) +
  geom_point(aes(fill = variable), shape = 21, col = "grey20") +
  scale_color_viridis_d() +
  scale_fill_viridis_d() +
  facet_grid(sat_level ~ biome, scales = "free_y")

saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_surface <-
saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_raw %>%
  group_by(tref, pCO2, biome, sat_level, MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask) %>% 
  summarise(area = sum(area)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  group_by(biome, sat_level, MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask) %>% 
  arrange(tref) %>% 
  mutate(area_change = 100 * (area - first(area)) / first(area),
         n = n()) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  filter(n == 4) %>% 
  select(-n)


saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_surface %>% 
  ggplot(aes(pCO2, area_change)) +
  geom_path(aes(group = interaction(MLR_configuration, MLR_basin_mask))) +
  facet_grid(sat_level ~ biome)

volume_total <-
  ocean_volume_integration_depth %>%
  filter(depth_integration == ocean_depth) %>%
  pull(volume_total)

acidification_volume <-
  undersaturated_volume_all %>%
  mutate(volume = volume_total - volume_undersat)

acidification_volume <-
  bind_rows(
    acidification_volume,
    expand_grid(
      acidification_volume %>%
        filter(
          MLR_basin_mask == MLR_basin_mask_reference,
          MLR_configuration == MLR_configuration_reference,
          tref == 1800
        ) %>%
        select(-c(MLR_basin_mask)),
      MLR_basin_mask = MLR_basin_mask_uncertainty
    ),
    expand_grid(
      acidification_volume %>%
        filter(
          MLR_basin_mask == MLR_basin_mask_reference,
          MLR_configuration == MLR_configuration_reference,
          tref == 1800
        ) %>%
        select(-c(MLR_configuration)),
      MLR_configuration = MLR_configuration_uncertainty
    )
  )


acidification_volume <-
  acidification_volume %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(sat_level, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  mutate(
    volume_loss =
      volume - lag(volume, default = first(volume)),
    volume_loss_relative_to_preind_volume =
      100 * volume_loss / first(volume),
    volume_loss_cumulative =
      volume - first(volume),
    volume_loss_cumulative_relative_to_preind_volume =
      100 * volume_loss_cumulative / first(volume),
    volume_relative_to_total_volume = 100 * volume / volume_total,
    volume_loss_relative_to_total_volume = 100 * volume_loss / volume_total,
    volume_loss_cumulative_relative_to_total_volume = 100 * volume_loss_cumulative / volume_total,
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

acidification_volume <-
  acidification_volume %>%
  select(-c(volume_undersat)) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("volume"),
               names_to = "estimate",
               values_to = "value")


acidification_volume <-
  acidification_volume %>%
  filter(
    estimate %in% c(
      "volume_relative_to_total_volume",
      "volume_loss_cumulative_relative_to_total_volume",
      "volume_loss_cumulative_relative_to_preind_volume"
    )
  )

acidification_volume <-
  additive_uncertainty(
    df = acidification_volume %>%
      mutate(estimate = paste0(estimate, "_interval_mean")) %>%
      pivot_wider(names_from = estimate,
                  values_from = value),
    mode = "delta_total"
  )[[1]]


acidification_volume <-
  right_join(co2_atm_reccap2 %>% rename(tref = year),
             acidification_volume)

co2_atm_level <- acidification_volume %>%
  distinct(pCO2) %>%
  pull() %>%
  round()

acidification_volume <-
  acidification_volume %>%
  rename(estimate = variable) %>%
  mutate(
    sat_level = as.factor(sat_level),
    estimate = case_when(
      estimate == "volume_relative_to_total_volume" ~
        "Saturated volume\nrelative to total volume (%)",
      estimate == "volume_loss_cumulative_relative_to_total_volume" ~
        "Loss of\nsatured volume\nrelative to total volume (%)",
      estimate == "volume_loss_cumulative_relative_to_preind_volume" ~
        "Loss of saturated volume\n\nrelative preindustrial volume (%)"
    ),
    estimate = factor(
      estimate,
      levels = c(
        "Saturated volume\nrelative to total volume (%)",
        "Loss of\nsatured volume\nrelative to total volume (%)",
        "Loss of saturated volume\n\nrelative preindustrial volume (%)"
      )
    )
  )


acidification_volume %>%
  filter(sat_level %in% c(1,2,3,4)) %>% 
  ggplot(aes(
    x = pCO2,
    y = std_case,
    ymin = std_case - sd,
    ymax = std_case + sd
  )) +
  labs(x = expression(Atmospheric ~ CO[2] ~ (ppm))) +
  scale_x_continuous(
    breaks = seq(280, 400, 40),
    sec.axis = sec_axis(
      ~ (. - 282.5) * 1.537,
      breaks = seq(0, 175, 50),

    )
  ) +
  geom_ribbon(aes(fill = sat_level),
              alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(col = sat_level, group = sat_level)) +
  geom_point(aes(fill = sat_level,
                 shape = sat_level)) +
  geom_text(
    data = . %>%
      filter(
        estimate == "Loss of saturated volume\n\nrelative preindustrial volume (%)",
        sat_level == 4,
        tref != 1800
      ),
    aes(label = tref),
    nudge_y = -7,
    nudge_x = -4
  ) +
  geom_text(
    data = . %>%
      filter(
        estimate == "Loss of saturated volume\n\nrelative preindustrial volume (%)",
        sat_level == 4,
        tref == 1800
      ),

    nudge_y = 7,
    nudge_x = 4
  ) +
  scale_color_viridis_d(name = expression(atop(Ω[arag], threshold)),
                        end = 0.9) +
  scale_fill_viridis_d(name = expression(atop(Ω[arag], threshold)),
                       end = 0.9) +
  scale_shape_manual(values = 21:27,
                     name = expression(atop(Ω[arag], threshold))) +
  theme(
    axis.title.y = element_blank(),
    legend.position = c(0.15, 0.47),
    legend.background = element_rect(fill = "transparent"),
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(estimate ~ .,
             scales = "free_y",
             switch = "y") +
  facetted_pos_scales(
    y = list(NULL, NULL, scale_y_continuous(limits = c(-100,0), expand = c(0.11,0.11)))
  )

Summary table

table_absolute_format <-
  table_absolute %>%
  filter(biome == "Global",
         tref != 2004) %>%
  mutate(std_case = case_when(
    variable %in% c("H_free", "OmegaAragonite", "pH") ~ round(std_case, 2),
    variable == "tco2" ~ round(std_case, 0)
  )) %>%
  mutate(value = paste(std_case, "±", signif(sd, 1))) %>%
  select(-c(sd, std_case, biome)) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = value)


table_incremental_change_format <-
  table_incremental_change %>%
  filter(biome == "Global") %>%
  mutate(std_case = case_when(
    variable %in% c("H_free", "OmegaAragonite") ~ round(std_case, 2),
    variable %in% c("pH") ~ round(std_case, 3),
    variable == "tco2" ~ round(std_case, 0)
  )) %>%
  mutate(value = paste(std_case, "±", signif(sd, 1))) %>%
  select(-c(sd, std_case, biome)) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = value)

table_rel_change_format <-
  table_rel_change %>%
  filter(biome == "Global",
         tref == 2014) %>%
  mutate(tref = "1994-2014 / 1800-1994") %>%
  mutate(value = paste(round(std_case, 0), "±", round(sd, 0), "%")) %>%
  select(-c(sd, std_case, biome)) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = value)

table_sat_horizon_format <- 
full_join(
  full_join(
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_change_combined %>%
      filter(biome == "Global",
             sat_level %in% c(1, 2, 3, 4)) %>%
      select(-c(depth_01, depth_025, tref, biome)) %>%
      pivot_wider(names_from = period,
                  values_from = depth) %>%
      rename(depth = sat_level) %>%
      mutate(variable = "sat_depth"),
    saturation_horizon_uncertainty_all_biome_combined %>%
      filter(biome == "Global",
             sat_level %in% c(1, 2, 3, 4),
             tref != 2004) %>%
      select(-c(depth_01, depth_025, biome)) %>%
      pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
                  values_from = depth) %>%
      rename(depth = sat_level) %>%
      mutate(variable = "sat_depth")
  ),
  table_sat_horizon_rel %>%
    filter(
      biome == "Global",
      sat_level %in% c(1, 2, 3, 4),
      tref == 2014,
      variable == "depth"
    ) %>%
    mutate("1994-2014 / 1800-1994" = paste(round(std_case, 0), "±", round(sd, 0), "%")) %>%
    select(-c(sd, std_case, biome, variable, tref)) %>%
    rename(depth = sat_level)
)

  
table_acidification_format <-   
full_join(
  full_join(table_absolute_format,
            table_incremental_change_format),
  table_rel_change_format
)

table_all <- 
bind_rows(
  table_acidification_format,
  table_sat_horizon_format %>% 
    mutate(depth = as.character(depth))
)


table_all %>% 
  write_csv(here::here("output/main/table1.csv"))

cwc_saturation_state <-
  inner_join(
    cwc %>% 
      distinct(lat, lon, DEPTH_MAX) %>% 
      mutate(obs_id = row_number()) %>%
      rename(depth = DEPTH_MAX),
    acidification_trend %>% distinct(lat, lon, tref),
    relationship = "many-to-many"
  )
  
cwc_saturation_state <-
  full_join(
    cwc_saturation_state,
    acidification_trend %>%
      select(tref, lon, lat, depth, OmegaAragonite)
  )


cwc_saturation_state <-
  cwc_saturation_state %>%
  arrange(depth) %>%
  group_by(lon, lat) %>%
  mutate(cwc_absence = all(is.na(obs_id))) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  filter(cwc_absence != TRUE) %>%
  select(-cwc_absence)


cwc_saturation_state <-
  cwc_saturation_state %>%
  arrange(lat, lon, tref, depth)


cwc_saturation_state <-
  cwc_saturation_state %>%
  group_by(lon, lat, tref) %>%
  mutate(OmegaAragonite =
           approxfun(depth,
                     OmegaAragonite,
                     rule = 1)(depth)) %>%
  ungroup() %>% 
  filter(!is.na(obs_id))

Zonal sections

Computation

acidification_zonal <- acidification_trend %>%
  group_by(tref) %>%
  nest() %>%
  mutate(zonal = map(.x = data, ~m_zonal_mean_sd(.x))) %>%
  select(-data) %>%
  unnest(zonal) %>% 
  ungroup()
acidification_zonal_dCant_temp <- dCant_temp_trend %>%
  group_by(tref, driver) %>%
  nest() %>%
  mutate(zonal = map(.x = data, ~m_zonal_mean_sd(.x))) %>%
  select(-data) %>%
  unnest(zonal) %>% 
  ungroup()
acidification_zonal_buffer <- buffer_trend %>%
  group_by(tref) %>%
  nest() %>%
  mutate(zonal = map(.x = data, ~m_zonal_mean_sd(.x))) %>%
  select(-data) %>%
  unnest(zonal) %>% 
  ungroup()

Incremental changes

dCant + Temperature

acidification_zonal_dCant_temp <-
  acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>%
  select(-contains("_sd")) %>% 
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_interval"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_interval") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_interval_mean"))

# create pdf document

pdf(
  here::here("output/all_variables/zonal_mean_sections_dCant_temp_changes.pdf"),
  width = 20,
  height = 6
)

# loop over OIA variables
# print incremental sections

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[10]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp <-
    acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  # determine endpoints and breaks of color scale
  
  low <- i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_interval)) %>%
    pull(delta_interval) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_low), names = FALSE)
  
  high <- i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_interval)) %>%
    pull(delta_interval) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_high), names = FALSE)
  
  breaks <- c(-Inf, seq(low, high, length.out = break_numbers), Inf)
  
  p_zonal_dcant_temp <-
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      df = i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>% 
        filter(driver == "dCant + temp"),
      var = "delta_interval",
      legend_title = i_var,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = breaks,
      title_text = "Driver: dCant + temp",
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    facet_grid(tref ~ basin_AIP)
  
  p_zonal_dcant <-
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      df = i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>% 
        filter(driver == "dCant"),
      var = "delta_interval",
      legend_title = i_var,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = breaks,
      title_text = "Driver: dCant",
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    facet_grid(tref ~ basin_AIP)

  p_decadal_offset <-
    i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>%
    arrange(depth, lat) %>%
    select(depth, lat, basin_AIP, tref, driver, delta_interval) %>%
    drop_na() %>%
    pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
                values_from = delta_interval) %>%
    mutate(delta_delta_interval = `2014` - `2004`) %>%
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      var = "delta_delta_interval",
      legend_title = paste0("delta\n",i_var),
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = NULL,
      col = "div",
      title_text = "Decadal difference",
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    facet_grid(driver ~ basin_AIP)

  p_temperature_offset <-
    i_acidification_zonal_dCant_temp %>%
    arrange(depth, lat) %>%
    select(depth, lat, basin_AIP, tref, driver, delta_interval) %>%
    drop_na() %>%
    pivot_wider(names_from = driver,
                values_from = delta_interval) %>%
    mutate(delta_delta_interval = `dCant + temp` - `dCant`) %>%
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      var = "delta_delta_interval",
      legend_title = paste0("delta\n",i_var),
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = NULL,
      col = "div",
      title_text = "Driver difference",
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    facet_grid(tref ~ basin_AIP)
  
  print(
    wrap_plots(
      p_zonal_dcant &
        theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
              axis.text.x = element_blank()),
      p_zonal_dcant_temp &
        theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
              axis.text.x = element_blank()),
      p_decadal_offset,
      p_temperature_offset,
      ncol = 2
    )
  )
  
}

dev.off()

rm(acidification_zonal_dCant_temp)

dCant

# subset incremental change sections

acidification_zonal_incremental <-
  acidification_zonal %>%
  select(MLR_basin_mask:basin_AIP,
         contains("_delta_interval"),
         -contains("_sd")) %>%
  filter(tref %in% c(2004, 2014))

# downscaling for uncertainty computation

acidification_zonal_uncertainty <-
  acidification_zonal_incremental %>%
  mutate(lat = as.numeric(as.character(cut(
    lat, seq(-90, 90, 10), seq(-85, 85, 10)
  ))),
  depth = as.numeric(as.character(cut(
    depth,
    c(seq(0, 500, 100), seq(1000, 10000, 500)),
    c(seq(50, 450, 100), seq(750, 10000, 500)),
    right = FALSE
  )))
  ) %>%
  group_by(across(-contains("_delta_interval"))) %>%
  summarise(across(everything(), mean)) %>%
  ungroup()

# compute uncertainty

acidification_zonal_uncertainty <-
  additive_uncertainty(acidification_zonal_uncertainty)

delta_acidification_zonal_uncertainty <- acidification_zonal_uncertainty[[3]]
acidification_zonal_uncertainty <- acidification_zonal_uncertainty[[1]]


# subset reference reconstruction

acidification_zonal_incremental <-
  acidification_zonal_incremental %>%
  filter(MLR_basin_mask == MLR_basin_mask_reference,
         MLR_configuration == MLR_configuration_reference) %>%
  select(-c(MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration)) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_interval"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_interval") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_interval_mean"))


# create pdf document

pdf(
  here::here("output/all_variables/zonal_mean_sections_incremental_changes.pdf"),
  width = 12,
  height = 8
)

# loop over OIA variables
# print incremental sections

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[1]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_acidification_zonal_incremental <-
    acidification_zonal_incremental %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  i_acidification_zonal_uncertainty = acidification_zonal_uncertainty %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)

  i_delta_acidification_zonal_uncertainty = delta_acidification_zonal_uncertainty %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  # determine endpoints and breaks of color scale
  
  low <- i_acidification_zonal_incremental %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_interval)) %>%
    pull(delta_interval) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_low), names = FALSE)
  
  high <- i_acidification_zonal_incremental %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_interval)) %>%
    pull(delta_interval) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_high), names = FALSE)
  
  breaks <- c(-Inf, seq(low, high, length.out = break_numbers), Inf)
  
  p_zonal_dec <-
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      df = i_acidification_zonal_incremental,
      var = "delta_interval",
      legend_title = i_var,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = breaks,
      title_text = NULL,
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = i_acidification_zonal_uncertainty %>% filter(signif_single == 0),
      aes(lat, depth),
      shape = 20,
      size = 1,
      col = "grey"
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = i_acidification_zonal_uncertainty %>% filter(signif_double == 0),
      aes(lat, depth),
      shape = 20,
      size = 0.1,
      col = "grey"
    ) +
    facet_grid(tref ~ basin_AIP)

  
  
  
  p_zonal_offset <-
    i_acidification_zonal_incremental %>%
    arrange(depth, lat) %>%
    select(depth, lat, basin_AIP, tref, delta_interval) %>%
    drop_na() %>%
    pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
                values_from = delta_interval) %>%
    mutate(delta_delta_interval = `2014` - `2004`) %>%
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      var = "delta_delta_interval",
      legend_title = paste0("delta\n",i_var),
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = NULL,
      col = "div",
      title_text = NULL,
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = i_acidification_zonal_uncertainty %>% filter(signif_single == 0),
      aes(lat, depth),
      shape = 20,
      size = 1
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = i_acidification_zonal_uncertainty %>% filter(signif_double == 0),
      aes(lat, depth),
      shape = 20,
      size = 0.1
    ) +
    facet_grid(. ~ basin_AIP)
  
  print(
    wrap_plots(
      p_zonal_dec &
        theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
              axis.text.x = element_blank()),
      p_zonal_offset,
      ncol = 1
    )
  )
  
}

dev.off()

rm(acidification_zonal_incremental,
   acidification_zonal_uncertainty,
   delta_acidification_zonal_uncertainty
   )

Total changes

# subset total change sections

acidification_zonal_total <-
  acidification_zonal %>%
  select(tref:basin_AIP,
         contains("_delta_total_mean")) %>%
  filter(tref != 1800)


# subset reference reconstruction

acidification_zonal_total <-
  acidification_zonal_total %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_total"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_total_mean"))


# create pdf document

pdf(
  here::here("output/all_variables/zonal_mean_sections_total_changes.pdf"),
  width = 10,
  height = 8
)

# loop over OIA variables
# print incremental sections

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[1]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_acidification_zonal_total <-
    acidification_zonal_total %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  # determine endpoints and breaks of color scale
  
  low <- i_acidification_zonal_total %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_total)) %>%
    pull(delta_total) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_low), names = FALSE)

  high <- i_acidification_zonal_total %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_total)) %>%
    pull(delta_total) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_high), names = FALSE)

  breaks <- c(-Inf, seq(low, high, length.out = break_numbers), Inf)
  breaks_sub <- breaks[seq(1, length(breaks), 3)]
  
  
  p_total_fill <-
    p_section_zonal_continous_depth(
      df = i_acidification_zonal_total,
      var = "delta_total",
      legend_title = i_var,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = breaks,
      title_text = NULL,
      subtitle_text = NULL
    ) +
    facet_grid(tref ~ basin_AIP) +
    geom_contour(
      data = i_acidification_zonal_total,
      aes(lat, depth, z = delta_total),
      col = "white",
      breaks = breaks_sub
    )
  
  p_total_contour <-
    i_acidification_zonal_total %>%
    mutate(tref = as.factor(tref)) %>%
    ggplot() +
    geom_contour(aes(lat, depth, z = delta_total,
                     col = tref),
                 breaks = breaks_sub) +
    scale_y_continuous(
      trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
      breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)),
      limits = c(params_global$inventory_depth_standard, 0),
      name = "Depth (m)"
    ) +
    scale_x_continuous(
      breaks = seq(-100, 100, 20),
      limits = c(-80, 65),
      name = "Latitude (°N)"
    ) +
    scale_color_brewer(palette = "YlGnBu") +
    coord_fixed(ratio = 1, expand = 0) +
    facet_grid(. ~ basin_AIP)
  
  print(
    wrap_plots(
      p_total_fill,
      p_total_contour,
      ncol = 1
    )
  )
  
}

dev.off()

rm(acidification_zonal_total,
   i_acidification_zonal_total)

Global sections

Computation

acidification_global_section <- acidification_trend %>%
  group_by(tref) %>%
  nest() %>%
  mutate(zonal = map(.x = data, ~m_section_global_mean_sd(.x))) %>%
  select(-data) %>%
  unnest(zonal) %>% 
  ungroup()

buffer_global_section <- buffer_trend_addition %>%
  # pivot_wider(names_from = variable,
  #             values_from = sensitivity) %>% 
  group_by(tref) %>%
  nest() %>%
  mutate(zonal = map(.x = data, ~m_section_global_mean_sd(.x))) %>%
  select(-data) %>%
  unnest(zonal) %>% 
  ungroup()

Incremental changes

# subset incremental change sections

acidification_global_section_incremental <-
  acidification_global_section %>%
  select(tref:band, dist,
         contains("_delta_interval"),
         -contains("_sd")) %>%
  filter(tref %in% c(2004, 2014))

# downscaling for uncertainty computation

acidification_global_section_uncertainty <-
  acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
  mutate(dist = as.numeric(as.character(cut(
    dist, seq(0, 50, 1), seq(0.5, 49.5, 1)
  ))),
  depth = as.numeric(as.character(cut(
    depth,
    c(seq(0, 500, 100), seq(1000, 10000, 500)),
    c(seq(50, 450, 100), seq(750, 10000, 500)),
    right = FALSE
  )))) %>%
  group_by(across(-contains("_delta_interval"))) %>%
  summarise(across(everything(), mean)) %>%
  ungroup()

# compute uncertainty

acidification_global_section_uncertainty <-
  additive_uncertainty(acidification_global_section_uncertainty)

delta_acidification_global_section_uncertainty <- acidification_global_section_uncertainty[[3]]
acidification_global_section_uncertainty <- acidification_global_section_uncertainty[[1]]


# subset reference reconstruction

acidification_global_section_incremental <-
  acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
  filter(MLR_basin_mask == MLR_basin_mask_reference,
         MLR_configuration == MLR_configuration_reference) %>%
  select(-c(MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration)) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_interval"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_interval") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_interval_mean"))


# create pdf document

pdf(
  here::here("output/all_variables/global_sections_incremental_changes.pdf"),
  width = 10,
  height = 12
)

# loop over OIA variables
# print incremental sections

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[1]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_acidification_global_section_incremental <-
    acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  # determine endpoints and breaks of color scale
  
  low <- i_acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_interval)) %>%
    pull(delta_interval) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_low), names = FALSE)
  
  high <- i_acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
    filter(!is.na(delta_interval)) %>%
    pull(delta_interval) %>%
    quantile(c(quantile_high), names = FALSE)
  
  breaks <- c(-Inf, seq(low, high, length.out = break_numbers), Inf)
  
  p_global_section_dec1 <-
    i_acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
    filter(tref == 2004) %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "delta_interval",
      legend_title = i_var,
      title_text = "A   1994 - 2004",
      df_uncertainty = acidification_global_section_uncertainty %>%
        filter(tref == 2004,
               variable == i_var),
      breaks = breaks,
      col_uncertainty = "grey",
      subtitle_text = NULL,
      plot_slabs = "n"
    ) &
    theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
          axis.text.x.bottom = element_blank())
  
  p_global_section_dec2 <-
    i_acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
    filter(tref == 2014) %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "delta_interval",
      title_text = "B   2004 - 2014",
      subtitle_text = NULL,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      df_uncertainty = acidification_global_section_uncertainty %>%
        filter(tref == 2014,
               variable == i_var),
      col_uncertainty = "grey",
      breaks = breaks
    ) &
    theme(legend.position = "none")
  
  p_global_section_offset <-
    i_acidification_global_section_incremental %>%
    arrange(depth, dist) %>%
    select(depth, dist, tref, delta_interval) %>%
    drop_na() %>%
    pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
                values_from = delta_interval) %>%
    mutate(delta_delta_interval = `2014` - `2004`) %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "delta_delta_interval",
      legend_title = paste("delta\n", i_var),
      df_uncertainty = delta_acidification_global_section_uncertainty %>%
        filter(variable == i_var),
      plot_slabs = "n",
      col = "div",
      title_text = "C   Decadal difference",
      subtitle_text = NULL
    )
  
  print(
    wrap_plots(
      p_global_section_dec1,
      p_global_section_dec2 &
        theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
              axis.text.x = element_blank()),
      p_global_section_offset &
        theme(axis.text.x.top = element_blank()),
      ncol = 1
    )
  )
  
}

               values_to = "mean") %>%
  mutate(name = str_remove(name, "_mean"))


acidification_global_section_total <-
  full_join(acidification_global_section_total,
            absolute_global_section_total)

rm(absolute_global_section_total)

# loop over OIA variables
# print incremental sections

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[3]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_acidification_global_section_total <-
    acidification_global_section_total %>%
    filter(name == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks(i_var)
  i_breaks        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_contour_level <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[2])
  i_contour_level_abs <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[4])
  i_legend_title  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])
  
  p_global_section_period1 <-
    i_acidification_global_section_total %>%
    filter(tref == 1994) %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "delta_total",
      title_text = "A   1800 - 1994",
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      col_scale = "RdPu",
      breaks = i_breaks,
      n_labels = 2,
      subtitle_text = NULL,
      plot_slabs = "n"
    )
  
  p_global_section_period2 <-
    i_acidification_global_section_total %>%
    filter(tref == 2004) %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "delta_total",
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      col_scale = "RdPu",
      title_text = "B   1800 - 2004",
      subtitle_text = NULL,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = i_breaks,
      n_labels = 2
    )
  
  p_global_section_period3 <-
    i_acidification_global_section_total %>%
    filter(tref == 2014) %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "delta_total",
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      col_scale = "RdPu",
      title_text = "C   1800 - 2014",
      subtitle_text = NULL,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      breaks = i_breaks,
      n_labels = 2
    )
  
  if(i_var == "tco2"){
    p_global_section_tco2 <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
  if(i_var == "H_free"){
    p_global_section_H_free <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
  if(i_var == "pH"){
    p_global_section_pH <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
  if(i_var == "OmegaAragonite"){
    p_global_section_OmegaAragonite <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
  
  print(
    wrap_plots(
      p_global_section_period1 &
        theme(axis.title.x = element_blank(),
              axis.text.x.bottom = element_blank()),
      p_global_section_period2 &
        theme(
          axis.title.x = element_blank(),
          axis.text.x = element_blank(),
          legend.position = "none"
        ),
      p_global_section_period3 &
        theme(axis.text.x.top = element_blank(),
              legend.position = "none"),
      ncol = 1
    )
  )
  
  ggsave(
    here::here(
      paste0(
        "output/all_variables/global_sections_",
        i_var,
        "_total_changes.png"
      )
    ),
    width = 6,
    height = 8,
    dpi = 600,
    bg = "white"
  )

for (i_var in OIA_variables) {
  # i_var <- OIA_variables[3]
  
  # subset OIA variable
  
  i_acidification_global_section_absolute <-
    acidification_global_section_absolute %>%
    filter(variable == i_var,
           depth <= 3000)
  
  all_labels_breaks <- labels_breaks_absolute(i_var)
  i_breaks        <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[1])
  i_legend_title  <- unlist(all_labels_breaks[3])

    i_contour_level <- c(#1950,
                         2200
                         )
    i_contour_level_abs <- i_contour_level
  }

    i_contour_level <- c(#5
      9
                         )
    i_contour_level_abs <- i_contour_level
  }

    i_contour_level <- c(#5
      8
                         )

  }

    i_contour_level <- c(1
                         # , 4
                         )
    i_contour_level_abs <- i_contour_level
  }
  
  
  p_global_section_period3 <-
    i_acidification_global_section_absolute %>%
    p_section_global(
      var = "2014",
      var_contour = "1800",
      legend_title = i_legend_title,
      contour_level = i_contour_level,
      contour_level_var = i_contour_level_abs,
      title_text = NULL,
      subtitle_text = NULL,
      plot_slabs = "n",
      col_contour = "white",
      breaks = i_breaks,
      n_labels = 2
    )
  
  if(i_var == "tco2"){
    p_global_section_tco2 <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
  if(i_var == "H_free"){
    p_global_section_H_free <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
  if(i_var == "pH"){
    p_global_section_pH <- p_global_section_period3
  }

    p_global_section_OmegaAragonite <- p_global_section_period3
  }
  
}

Profiles

Computation

# join with 3D acidification fields

acidification_profiles <-
  full_join(basinmask,
            acidification_trend %>%
              select(-contains("temp"))) %>%
  drop_na() %>%
  relocate(tref)


# calculate regional means

acidification_profiles_regional <-
acidification_profiles %>% 
  group_by(tref, basin, depth) %>%
  summarise(across(
    .cols = tco2:H_free_delta_interval,
    .fns = ~ wmean(.x, area),
    .names = "{.col}-mean"
  ),
  across(
    .cols = tco2:H_free_delta_interval,
    .fns = ~ wsd(.x, area),
    .names = "{.col}-sd"
  )) %>%
  ungroup()

# calculate global means

acidification_profiles_global <- acidification_profiles %>%
  mutate(basin = "Global") %>%
  group_by(tref, basin, depth) %>%
  summarise(
    across(
      .cols = tco2:H_free_delta_interval,
      .fns = ~ wmean(.x, area),
      .names = "{.col}-mean"
    ),
    across(
      .cols = tco2:H_free_delta_interval,
      .fns = ~ wsd(.x, area),
      .names = "{.col}-sd"
    )
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

# join global and regional profiles
  
acidification_profiles <-
  bind_rows(acidification_profiles_global,
            acidification_profiles_regional)
  
rm(acidification_profiles_regional,
   acidification_profiles_global)


acidification_profiles <- acidification_profiles %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref))

  pivot_longer(-c(tref:depth))

ggsave(
  here::here(
    paste0(
      "output/supplement/profiles_total_changes_biome.png"
    )
  ),
  width = 8,
  height = 10,
  dpi = 600,
  bg = "white"
)
lat_lon_radius <- 3

TS_product <-
  bind_rows(ALOHA,
            BATS)

TS_product_stations <-
  TS_product %>%
  group_by(station) %>%
  summarise(lat_centre = mean(lat),
            lon_centre = mean(lon)) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  mutate(
    lat_south = case_when(
      station == "BATS" ~ lat_centre - lat_lon_radius,
      station == "ALOHA" ~ lat_centre
    ),
    lat_north = case_when(
      station == "BATS" ~ lat_centre,
      station == "ALOHA" ~ lat_centre + lat_lon_radius
    ),
    lon_east = case_when(
      station == "BATS" ~ lon_centre - lat_lon_radius / 2,
      station == "ALOHA" ~ lon_centre
    ),
    lon_west = case_when(
      station == "BATS" ~ lon_centre + lat_lon_radius / 2,
      station == "ALOHA" ~ lon_centre + lat_lon_radius
    )
  )



for (i_station in unique(TS_product_stations$station)) {
  # i_station <- unique(TS_product_stations$station)[1]
  
  i_TS_product_stations <- TS_product_stations %>%
    filter(station == i_station)
  
  acidification_profiles_station <-
    cross_join(i_TS_product_stations,
               acidification_trend)
  
  
  acidification_profiles_station <-
    acidification_profiles_station %>%
    filter(between(lat, lat_south, lat_north),
           between(lon, lon_east, lon_west)) %>%
    select(-contains("centre"))
  
  if (exists("acidification_profiles_station_all")) {
    acidification_profiles_station_all <-
      bind_rows(acidification_profiles_station_all,
                acidification_profiles_station)
  }
  
  if (!exists("acidification_profiles_station_all")) {
    acidification_profiles_station_all <-
      acidification_profiles_station
  }
  
}

acidification_profiles_station <-
  acidification_profiles_station_all
rm(acidification_profiles_station_all)

map +
  geom_tile(
    data = acidification_profiles_station %>%
      group_by(station, lat, lon) %>%
      summarise(depth = max(depth)) %>%
      ungroup(),
    aes(lon, lat, fill = depth)
  ) +
  scale_fill_viridis_c(direction = -1) +
  geom_tile(data = TS_product_stations,
            aes(lon_centre, lat_centre, width = 1, height = 1),
            fill = "red")


# determine 20 year changes

acidification_profiles_station <-
  acidification_profiles_station %>%
  filter(tref %in% c(1994, 2014)) %>%
  select(station, tref, lon, lat, depth,
         all_of(OIA_variables)) %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(station, lat, lon, depth) %>%
  mutate(across(where(is.numeric), ~ .x - first(.x))) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  filter(tref == 20) %>%
  mutate(tref = "reconstruction\n1994-2014")

  
# calculate regional means

acidification_profiles_station <- acidification_profiles_station %>%
  select(-c(lon, lat)) %>%
  group_by(tref, station, depth) %>%
  summarise(across(where(is.numeric),
                   ~ mean(.x))) %>%
  ungroup()

acidification_profiles_station <- acidification_profiles_station %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref))
# compute total temperature contribution to changes from 1994 to 2004 and 2014

dCant_temp_trend_temp_contribution <- dCant_temp_trend %>% 
  select(lon, lat, depth, tref, driver, contains("delta_interval")) %>% 
  pivot_longer(contains("delta_interval"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_interval") %>% 
  pivot_wider(values_from = delta_interval,
              names_from = driver) %>% 
  mutate(delta_interval_temp = `dCant + temp` - dCant) %>% 
  select(-contains("dcant")) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = delta_interval_temp) %>% 
  mutate(`2014` = `2014` + `2004`,
         variable = str_replace(variable, "delta_interval", "delta_total")) %>% 
  pivot_longer(c(`2014`, `2004`),
               names_to = "tref",
               values_to = "delta_total_temp") %>% 
  pivot_wider(names_from = variable,
              values_from = delta_total_temp)
  

# join with 3D acidification fields

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution <-
  full_join(basinmask,
            dCant_temp_trend_temp_contribution)

# scale values to surface area

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution <- dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution %>% 
  mutate(across(contains("_delta"),
                ~ . * area))

# calculate regional means

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_regional <- dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution %>%
  group_by(tref, basin, depth) %>%
  summarise(across(contains("_delta"),
                   ~ sum(.) / sum(area))) %>%
  ungroup()

# calculate global means

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_global <- dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution %>%
  mutate(basin = "Global") %>% 
  group_by(tref, basin, depth) %>%
  summarise(across(contains("_delta"),
                   ~ sum(.) / sum(area))) %>%
  ungroup()

# join global and regional profiles
  
dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution <-
  bind_rows(dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_global,
            dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_regional)
  
rm(dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_regional,
   dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_global)

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution <- dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref))

  select(tref,
         basin,
         depth,
         contains("_delta_total")) %>%

         depth <= 3000,

    legend.title = element_blank(),

    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(
    basin ~ variable,
    scales = "free",
    switch = "x",
    labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels)
  ) +
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                     breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))
