buffer_profiles <-
  full_join(basinmask,
            buffer_trend %>% select(-basin_AIP))

# scale values to surface area

buffer_profiles <- buffer_profiles %>% 
  mutate(across(gammaDIC:tco2_talk_ratio_delta_interval,
                ~ . * area))

# calculate regional means

buffer_profiles_regional <- buffer_profiles %>%
  group_by(tref, basin, depth) %>%
  summarise(across(gammaDIC:tco2_talk_ratio_delta_interval,
                   ~ sum(.) / sum(area))) %>%
  ungroup()

# calculate global means

buffer_profiles_global <- buffer_profiles %>%
  mutate(basin = "Global") %>% 
  group_by(tref, basin, depth) %>%
  summarise(across(gammaDIC:tco2_talk_ratio_delta_interval,
                   ~ sum(.) / sum(area))) %>%
  ungroup()

# join global and regional profiles
  
buffer_profiles <-
  bind_rows(buffer_profiles_global,
            buffer_profiles_regional)
  
rm(buffer_profiles_regional,
   buffer_profiles_global)


# rename basins

buffer_profiles <- buffer_profiles %>%
  mutate(
    basin = str_replace(basin,
                        "_",
                        ". "),
    basin = fct_relevel(
      basin,
      "Global",
      "N. Pacific",
      "N. Atlantic",
      "Indian",
      "S. Pacific",
      "S. Atlantic"
    )
  )

buffer_profiles <- buffer_profiles %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref))
# join with 3D acidification fields

buffer_profiles_biome <-
  inner_join(biomemask,
             buffer_trend_addition_uncertainty)

# calculate regional means

buffer_profiles_biome_regional <- buffer_profiles_biome %>%
  group_by(tref, biome, depth, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  summarise(
    across(
      .cols = all_of(buffer_variables_addition),
      .fns = ~ wmean(.x, area),
      .names = "{.col}_interval_mean"
      
    )
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

# calculate global means

buffer_profiles_biome_global <- buffer_profiles_biome %>%
  mutate(biome = "Global") %>%
  group_by(tref, biome, depth, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  summarise(
    across(
      .cols = all_of(buffer_variables_addition),
      .fns = ~ wmean(.x, area),
      .names = "{.col}_interval_mean"
      
    )
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

# join global and regional profiles
  
buffer_profiles_biome <-
  bind_rows(buffer_profiles_biome_global,
            buffer_profiles_biome_regional)
  
rm(buffer_profiles_biome_regional,
   buffer_profiles_biome_global)

buffer_profiles_biome <-
  additive_uncertainty(df = buffer_profiles_biome,
                       mode = "absolute",
                       cant_sigma = 2)[[1]]
# join with 3D acidification fields

acidification_profiles_biome_absolute <-
  inner_join(biomemask,
             acidification_trend_uncertainty_absolute)

acidification_profiles_biome_absolute <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  mutate(shell_dissolution = -66.29 * log(OmegaAragonite) + 61.21)

# calculate regional means

acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_regional <- 
  acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  group_by(tref, biome, depth, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  summarise(
    across(
      .cols = all_of(c(buffer_variables_addition, "shell_dissolution")),
      .fns = ~ wmean(.x, area),
      .names = "{.col}_interval_mean"
      
    )
  ) %>%
  ungroup()

# calculate global means

acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_global <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  mutate(biome = "Global") %>%
  group_by(tref, biome, depth, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  summarise(across(
    .cols = all_of(c(buffer_variables_addition, "shell_dissolution")),
    .fns = ~ wmean(.x, area),
    .names = "{.col}_interval_mean"
    
  )) %>%
  ungroup()

# join global and regional profiles
  
acidification_profiles_biome_absolute <-
  bind_rows(acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_global,
            acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_regional)
  
rm(acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_regional,
   acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_global)


# change in shell dissolution

acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_change <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(biome, depth, MLR_basin_mask, MLR_configuration) %>%
  mutate(across(contains("interval_mean"), ~ .x - first(.x))) %>%
  ungroup()



acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_change_test <-
  additive_uncertainty(df = acidification_profiles_biome_absolute_change)[[1]]

acidification_profiles_biome_absolute <-
  additive_uncertainty(df = acidification_profiles_biome_absolute,
                       mode = "absolute",
                       cant_sigma = 2)[[1]]

p_acid_profiles_global <-
  DIC_dCant_temp_profiles_biome %>%
  filter(biome == "Global",
         variable %in% c("OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2", "temp")) %>%

    "OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2", "temp"
  ))) %>%
  ggplot() +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, col = "grey") +
  geom_path(
    data = . %>% filter(variable == "temp"),
    aes(delta_interval,

        linetype = temperature)
  ) +

    data = . %>% filter(variable != "temp"),

acidification_profiles_biomes_uncertainty_interval %>%
  filter(depth <= 1000,
         variable %in% c("OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2")) %>%
  select(-sd) %>% 
  pivot_wider(names_from = tref,
              values_from = std_case) %>% 
  mutate(std_case = 100 * (`2004` + `2014`) / `1994`) %>% 
  group_by(biome, variable) %>% 
  summarise(sd = sd(std_case),
            std_case = mean(std_case))

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_long <-
dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution %>%
  select(tref,
         basin,
         depth,
         contains("_delta_total")) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_total"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total_temp") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_total")) %>%
  filter(depth <= 3000,
         variable %in% OIA_variables)

acidification_profiles_long <-
acidification_profiles %>%
  select(tref,
         basin,
         depth,
         contains("_delta_total")) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_total"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_total")) %>%
  filter(tref != 1800,
         depth <= 3000,
         variable %in% OIA_variables)


acidification_profiles_long_relative <-
  acidification_profiles_long %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  group_by(basin, depth, variable) %>%
  mutate(delta_total_relative = 100 * (delta_total - first(delta_total)) / first(delta_total)) %>%
  ungroup()

full_join(acidification_profiles_long,
          dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_long) %>% 
  replace_na(list(delta_total = 0, delta_total_temp = 0))

  mutate(delta_total_temp = delta_total + delta_total_temp)

                                           breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))
                      ), 6))

             labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels))

acidification_profiles_long_relative %>%
  filter(depth <= 500) %>%
  group_by(basin, variable, tref) %>%
  summarise(delta_total_relative = mean(delta_total_relative)) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  mutate(tref = as.numeric(as.character(tref))) %>%
  arrange(tref) %>%
  ggplot(aes(tref, delta_total_relative, col = basin)) +
  geom_path() +
  geom_point(shape = 21, fill = "white") +
  scale_color_okabeito() +
  scale_x_continuous(breaks = seq(1994, 2014, 10)) +
  labs(y = "ΔOIA top 500m (% relative to 1994 OIA)") +
  theme(
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_markdown(),
        legend.position = c(0.8,0.25)
  ) +
  facet_wrap( ~ variable,
              labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels))

Biomes

dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_biome_long <-
dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_biome %>%
  select(tref,
         biome,
         depth,
         contains("_delta_total")) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_total"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total_temp") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_total")) %>%
  filter(depth <= 3000,
         variable %in% OIA_variables)

acidification_profiles_biome_long <-
acidification_profiles_biomes %>%
  select(tref,
         biome,
         depth,
         contains("_delta_total")) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_total"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_total") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_total")) %>%
  filter(tref != 1800,
         depth <= 3000,
         variable %in% OIA_variables)

acidification_profiles_biome_long <-
full_join(acidification_profiles_biome_long,
          dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_biome_long) %>% 
  replace_na(list(delta_total = 0, delta_total_temp = 0))

acidification_profiles_biome_long <- acidification_profiles_biome_long %>% 
  mutate(delta_total_temp = delta_total + delta_total_temp)



p_acid_profiles_global <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_long %>%
  filter(biome == "Global",
         variable %in% c("OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2", "temp")) %>%
  mutate(variable = factor(variable, levels = c(
    "OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2", "temp"
  ))) %>%
  ggplot() +
  geom_path(aes(delta_total_temp,
                depth,
                col = tref, linetype = "dcant_temp"),
                linewidth = 0.8) +
  geom_path(
    data = . %>% filter(variable != "temp"),
    aes(delta_total,
        depth,
        col = tref, linetype = "dcant_only"),
    linewidth = 0.8
  ) +
  scale_color_manual(values = three_year_colors) +
  scale_linetype_manual(values = c(1, 2),
                        labels = c(expression(Delta * C[ant]),
                                   expression(atop(Delta * C[ant] ~ "+", Temp)))) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       title = "Global") +
  theme(
    legend.position = "none",
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_markdown(),
    legend.key.width = unit(1, "cm")
  ) +
  facet_wrap(. ~ variable,
             scales = "free_x",
             labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels)
             ) +
  facetted_pos_scales(#x = x_axis_scales,
    y = rep(list(
      scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                         breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))
    ), 6))

acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval <-
acidification_profiles_biomes %>%
  select(tref,
         biome,
         depth,
         contains("_delta_interval")) %>%
  pivot_longer(contains("_delta_interval"),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_interval") %>%
  mutate(variable = str_remove(variable, "_delta_interval")) %>%
  filter(tref %in% c(2004, 2014),
         depth <= 3000,
         variable %in% OIA_variables)


acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval <-
  full_join(
    acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval,
    dCant_temp_profiles_temp_contribution_biome_long %>%
      group_by(biome, depth, variable) %>%
      mutate(delta_interval_temp = delta_total_temp - lag(delta_total_temp, default = 0)) %>%
      ungroup() %>% 
      select(-delta_total_temp)
  ) %>%
  replace_na(list(delta_interval = 0, delta_interval_temp = 0))


acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval %>%
  mutate(delta_interval_temp = delta_interval + delta_interval_temp)



acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval %>%
    group_by(biome, depth, variable) %>% 
    mutate(tref = paste0(lag(tref, default = "1994"), "-", tref)) %>% 
    ungroup()

p_acid_profiles_global <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval %>%
  filter(biome == "Global",
         variable %in% c("OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2", "temp")) %>%
  mutate(variable = factor(variable, levels = c(
    "OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2", "temp"
  ))) %>%
  ggplot() +
  geom_path(aes(delta_interval_temp,
                depth,
                col = tref, linetype = "dcant_temp"),
                linewidth = 0.8) +
  geom_path(
    data = . %>% filter(variable != "temp"),
    aes(delta_interval,
        depth,
        col = tref, linetype = "dcant_only"),
    linewidth = 0.8
  ) +
  scale_color_manual(values = two_year_colors) +
  scale_linetype_manual(values = c(1, 2),
                        labels = c(expression(Delta * C[ant]),
                                   expression(atop(Delta * C[ant] ~ "+", Temp)))) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       title = "Global") +
  theme(
    legend.position = "none",
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_markdown(),
    legend.key.width = unit(1, "cm")
  ) +
  facet_wrap(. ~ variable,
             scales = "free_x",
             labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels)
             ) +
  scale_x_continuous(guide = guide_axis(n.dodge = 2)) +
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                         breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))

acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval <-
  acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval %>%
  mutate(delta_interval_rel_temp = (100 * delta_interval_temp / delta_interval) -
           100)


acidification_profiles_biome_long_interval %>%
  filter(depth <= 1000) %>%
  group_by(tref, biome, variable) %>%
  summarise(temp_enhance = mean(delta_interval_rel_temp),
            temp_enhance_sd = sd(delta_interval_rel_temp)) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  arrange(biome, variable, tref) %>% 
  kable() %>%
  kable_styling() %>%
  scroll_box(height = "300px")

  ungroup() %>%
  arrange(biome, variable) %>% 
  kable() %>%
  kable_styling() %>%
  scroll_box(height = "300px")

p_ptero_abs <- 
acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  filter(depth <= 500,
         variable == "shell_dissolution") %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref),
         std_case = if_else(std_case < 0, 0, std_case)) %>% 
  filter(biome %in% c("Southern\nOcean", "Upwelling\nregions"),
         tref != 2004) %>% 
  ggplot() +
  geom_ribbon(aes(
    xmin = std_case - sd,
    xmax = std_case + sd,
    y = depth,
    fill = tref
  ), alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(std_case,
                depth,
                col = tref, 
                linewidth = tref)) +
  scale_color_manual(values = four_year_colors[c(1,2,4)]) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = four_year_colors[c(1,2,4)]) +
  scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(0.5,rep(1,3))) +
  scale_y_reverse(expand = c(0,0)) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       x = "Pteropod shell dissolution (%)") +
  theme(legend.title = element_blank(),
        legend.position = c(0.88,0.85),
        legend.background = element_rect(fill = "transparent"),
        axis.title.x = element_markdown()) +
  facet_wrap(~ biome)

p_ptero_change <-
acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  filter(depth <= 500,
         variable == "shell_dissolution") %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref),
         std_case = if_else(std_case < 0, 0, std_case)) %>% 
  group_by(biome, depth, variable) %>%
  mutate(std_case = std_case - first(std_case)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  filter(biome %in% c("Southern\nOcean", "Upwelling\nregions"),
         tref %in% c(1994, 2014)) %>% 
  ggplot() +
  geom_ribbon(aes(
    xmin = std_case - sd,
    xmax = std_case + sd,
    y = depth,
    fill = tref
  ), alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(std_case,
                depth,
                col = tref, 
                linewidth = tref)) +
  scale_color_manual(values = three_year_colors[c(1,3)]) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = three_year_colors[c(1, 3)]) +
  scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(0.5, rep(1, 3))) +
  scale_y_reverse(expand = c(0, 0)) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       x = "Δ Pteropod shell dissolution since 1800 (%)") +
  theme(
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    legend.position = "none",
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_wrap( ~ biome)

    xmin = std_case - sd,

                depth,

  ) +

p_ptero_abs <-
acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  filter(depth <= 500,
         variable == "shell_dissolution") %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref),
         std_case = if_else(std_case < 0, 0, std_case)) %>% 
  filter(biome %in% c("Southern\nOcean", "Upwelling\nregions"),
         tref != 2004) %>% 
  ggplot() +
  geom_ribbon(aes(
    xmin = std_case - sd,
    xmax = std_case + sd,
    y = depth,
    fill = tref
  ), alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(std_case,
                depth,
                col = tref, 
                linewidth = tref)) +
  scale_color_manual(values = four_year_colors[c(1,2,4)]) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = four_year_colors[c(1,2,4)]) +
  scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(0.5,rep(1,3))) +
  scale_y_reverse(expand = c(0,0)) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       x = "Shell diss. (%)") +
  theme(
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    legend.position = c(0.3, 0.15),
    legend.background = element_rect(fill = "transparent"),
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.text = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(biome ~ .)

p_ptero_change <-
acidification_profiles_biome_absolute %>%
  filter(depth <= 500,
         variable == "shell_dissolution") %>%
  mutate(tref = as.factor(tref),
         std_case = if_else(std_case < 0, 0, std_case)) %>% 
  group_by(biome, depth, variable) %>%
  mutate(std_case = std_case - first(std_case)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  filter(biome %in% c("Southern\nOcean", "Upwelling\nregions"),
         tref %in% c(1994, 2014)) %>% 
  ggplot() +
  geom_ribbon(aes(
    xmin = std_case - sd,
    xmax = std_case + sd,
    y = depth,
    fill = tref
  ), alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(std_case,
                depth,
                col = tref, 
                linewidth = tref)) +
  scale_color_manual(values = three_year_colors[c(1,3)]) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = three_year_colors[c(1, 3)]) +
  scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(0.5, rep(1, 3))) +
  scale_y_reverse(expand = c(0, 0)) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       x = "Δ Shell diss. (%)") +
  theme(
    axis.title.y = element_blank(),
    axis.text.y = element_blank(),
    legend.position = "none",
    legend.background = element_rect(fill = "transparent"),
    strip.background = element_blank(),
    strip.text = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(biome ~ .)

acidification_profiles %>%
  select(tref,
         basin,
         depth,
         # MLR_basin_mask,
         # MLR_configuration,
         all_of(OIA_variables)) %>%
  pivot_longer(-c(tref:depth),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "total") %>%
  filter(depth <= 3000) %>%
  ggplot(aes(
    total,
    depth,
    col = tref
  )) +
  geom_path() +
  scale_color_brewer(palette = "YlGnBu") +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       title = "Absolute state at reference years")+
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                     breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000))) +
  theme(legend.title = element_blank(),
        axis.title.x = element_blank()) +
  facet_grid(basin ~ variable, scales = "free_x")

dev.off()


acidification_profiles %>%
  filter(depth <= 3000,
         variable == "OmegaAragonite") %>%
  ggplot() +
  geom_vline(xintercept = c(1, 1.5, 2, 3, 4),
             linewidth = 0.2) +
  geom_ribbon(data = . %>% filter(tref == 1800),
              aes(xmax = mean + sd,
                  xmin = mean - sd,
                  y = depth,
                  fill = tref),
              alpha = 0.2) +
  geom_path(aes(mean,
                depth,
                col = tref), linewidth = 1) +
  scale_color_viridis_d(option = "plasma",
                        begin = 0,
                        end = 0.8) +
  scale_fill_viridis_d(option = "plasma",
                        begin = 0,
                        end = 0.8) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)",
       title = "Absolute state at reference years") +
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                     breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000))) +
  theme(legend.title = element_blank(),
        axis.title.x = element_blank()) +
  facet_wrap( ~ basin, scales = "free_x")

p_acid_profiles_global_omega <-
  acidification_profiles_biomes_uncertainty %>%
  filter(biome == "Global",
         variable %in% c("OmegaAragonite")) %>%
  mutate(variable = factor(variable, levels = c("OmegaAragonite", "H_free", "tco2"))) %>%
  ggplot() +
  geom_ribbon(aes(
    xmin = std_case - sd,
    xmax = std_case + sd,
    y = depth,
    fill = tref
  ),
  alpha = 0.3) +
  geom_path(aes(std_case,
                depth,
                col = tref,
                linewidth = tref)) +
  scale_color_manual(values = four_year_colors) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = four_year_colors) +
  scale_discrete_manual("linewidth", values = c(0.5,rep(1,3))) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)") +
  theme(
    axis.title = element_blank(),
    axis.text.y = element_blank(),
    strip.text.x = element_markdown(),
    legend.position = "none",
    legend.key.width = unit(1, "cm"),
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    strip.background.x = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside"
  ) +
  facet_wrap(
    . ~ variable,
    scales = "free_x",
    labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels),
    strip.position = "bottom",
    ncol = 1
  ) +
  scale_y_continuous(
    trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
    breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)),
    limits = c(3000, 0),
    expand = c(0, 0)
  )

    xmin = std_case - sd,
    xmax = std_case + sd,

Time series stations

TS_product <- TS_product %>%
  group_by(across(-value)) %>%
  summarise(value = mean(value, na.rm = TRUE)) %>%
  ungroup() %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = name,
              values_from = value) %>%
  filter(!is.na(tco2),
         !is.na(talk),
         !is.na(sal),
         !is.na(temp)) 


TS_product <-
  TS_product %>%
  group_by(station, depth_int) %>%
  mutate(across(PO4:talk,
                ~ mean(.x, na.rm = TRUE),
                .names = "{.col}_mean")) %>%
  ungroup()


TS_product_tco2_star_talk <-
  TS_product %>%
  mutate(tco2 =
           tco2  -
           0.5 * ((talk - talk_mean) + (16 * (PO4 - PO4_mean)))) %>%
  filter(!is.na(tco2)) %>%
  select(-talk) %>%
  rename(talk = talk_mean)

TS_product_tco2_star_talk_PO4 <-
  TS_product_tco2_star_talk %>%
  mutate(tco2 =
           tco2  -
           (117 * (PO4 - PO4_mean))) %>%
  filter(!is.na(tco2)) %>% 
  select(-PO4) %>% 
  rename(PO4 = PO4_mean)

TS_product_mean <- TS_product


TS_product <-
  bind_rows(
    TS_product %>% mutate(DIC_variant = "tco2"),
    TS_product_tco2_star_talk %>% mutate(DIC_variant = "tco2_star_talk"),
    TS_product_tco2_star_talk_PO4 %>% mutate(DIC_variant = "tco2_star_talk_PO4")
  ) %>% 
  select(-contains("mean"))

rm(TS_product_tco2_star_talk,
   TS_product_tco2_star_talk_PO4)

TS_product <-
  TS_product %>%
  # head(10) %>%
  mutate(
    sir(
      flag = 15,
      var1 = talk * 1e-6,
      var2 = tco2 * 1e-6,
      S = sal,
      T = temp,
      P = depth / 10,
      # Pt = phosphate * 1e-6,
      # Sit = silicate * 1e-6,
      k1k2 = "s20",
      kf = "dg",
      pHscale = "T"
    )[c(6, 18, 20, 21)]
  )


TS_product <-
  TS_product %>%
  mutate(across(contains("H_free"), ~ . * 1e3))

TS_product <-
  TS_product %>%
  relocate(DIC_variant, .before = PO4) %>% 
  pivot_longer(PO4:H_free)

date_range <-
  c(min(TS_product$date),
    max(TS_product$date))



TS_product %>% 
  filter(!is.na(value),
         depth <= 3000) %>% 
  ggplot(aes(value, depth, col = year)) +
  geom_point(size = 1, alpha = 0.5) +
  scale_color_viridis_c() +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)") +
  theme(
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.background.x = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_nested(
    station + DIC_variant ~ name,
    scales = "free",
    switch = "x",
    labeller = labeller(name = x_axis_labels_stations_absolute)
  ) +
  scale_x_continuous(guide = guide_axis(n.dodge = 2)) +
  facetted_pos_scales(y = rep(list(
    scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                       breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))
  ), 6))

      ) +

      )
  )

detrended <- TS_product %>%
  nest(data = -c(depth_int, station, name, DIC_variant)) %>%
  mutate(
    fit = map(data, ~ lm(value ~ date, data = .x)),
    tidied = map(fit, tidy),
    glanced = map(fit, glance),
    augmented = map(fit, augment)
  )

  unnest(augmented) %>% 
  select(station, name, depth_int, DIC_variant, date, value, value_detrended = .resid)

regressions <- detrended %>%
  nest(data = -c(station, depth_int, name, DIC_variant)) %>%
  mutate(
    fit = map(data, ~ lm(value_deseason ~ year, data = .x)),
    tidied = map(fit, tidy),
    glanced = map(fit, glance),
    augmented = map(fit, augment)
  )

TS_trends <- 
regressions %>%
  unnest(tidied) %>%
  arrange(depth_int) %>%
  filter(term == "year",
         depth_int <= 3000)



TS_trends %>%
  filter(station == "ALOHA" | depth_int <= 500) %>% 
  ggplot(aes(estimate, depth_int)) +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0) +
  geom_ribbon(aes(
    xmin = estimate - std.error,
    xmax = estimate + std.error,
    fill = DIC_variant
  ),
  alpha = 0.5) +
  geom_path(aes(col = DIC_variant)) +
  scale_fill_brewer(palette = "Dark2") +
  scale_color_brewer(palette = "Dark2") +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)") +
  theme(
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.background.x = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(
    station ~ name,
    scales = "free_x",
    switch = "x",
    labeller = labeller(name = x_axis_labels_stations)
  ) +
  scale_x_continuous(guide = guide_axis(n.dodge = 2)) +
  facetted_pos_scales(y = rep(list(
    scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                       breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))
  ), 6))

# ggsave(
#   here::here("output/supplement/BATS_ALOHA_all_variables_profiles_trend.png"),
#   width = 14,
#   height = 10
# )
acidification_profiles_station <-
  acidification_profiles_station %>%
  pivot_longer(-c(tref:depth),
               names_to = "variable",
               values_to = "delta_interval") %>%
  filter(depth <= ocean_depth)

acidification_profiles_station <- acidification_profiles_station %>%
  filter(variable %in% OIA_variables)

acidification_profiles_station_obs_reconstructed <-
  bind_rows(
    TS_trends %>%
      filter(term == "year") %>%
      select(
        station,
        DIC_variant,
        variable = name,
        depth = depth_int,
        estimate,
        std.error
      ) %>%
      mutate(
        driver = "observed",
        tref = "trend over\nobserved\nperiod",
        delta_interval = estimate * 20,
        std.error = std.error * 20
      ),
    acidification_profiles_station %>%
      mutate(DIC_variant = "tco2_star_talk_PO4",
             driver = "reconstructed")
  )


acidification_profiles_station_obs_reconstructed %>%
  filter(station == "ALOHA" & depth <= 250 |
           station == "BATS" & depth <= 500) %>% 
  group_by(station, variable, driver, DIC_variant) %>% 
  summarise(delta_interval = mean(delta_interval)) %>% 
  ungroup() %>% 
  pivot_wider(names_from = driver,
              values_from = delta_interval) %>% 
  mutate(relative = 100 * reconstructed / observed) %>% 
  drop_na()

labels_tco2 <- c(
  "DIC",
  "DIC*(TA)",
  "DIC*(TA,P)"
)

# colors_accent <- c("#D9DB95", "#DCA99E", "#033F63")
colors_accent <- c("grey80", "grey50", "#AA4499")

acidification_profiles_station_obs_reconstructed %>%
  filter(
    station == "ALOHA" | depth <= 500 | driver == "reconstructed",
    variable %in% c("tco2", "H_free", "OmegaAragonite")
  ) %>%
  mutate(variable = factor(
    variable,
    levels = c("H_free", "OmegaAragonite", "tco2",
               "talk", "PO4", "temp", "sal")
  )) %>%
  ggplot(aes(delta_interval,
             depth)) +
  geom_ribbon(
    data = . %>% filter(
      !is.na(std.error),
      variable %in% c("H_free", "OmegaAragonite", "tco2")
    ),
    aes(
      xmin = delta_interval - std.error,
      xmax = delta_interval + std.error,
      fill = DIC_variant
    ),
    alpha = 0.2
  ) +
  geom_path(
    data = . %>% filter(variable %in% c("H_free", "OmegaAragonite", "tco2")),
    aes(
      col = DIC_variant,
      linetype = driver,
    )
  ) +
  scale_fill_manual(values = colors_accent,
                    labels = labels_tco2) +
  scale_color_manual(values = colors_accent,
                     labels = labels_tco2) +
  scale_discrete_manual("linewidth",
                        labels = labels_tco2,
                        values = c(0.3, 0.3, 1)) +
  scale_linetype_manual(values = c(73,"solid")) +
  scale_x_continuous() +
  guides(
    colour = guide_legend(order = 1),
    fill = guide_legend(order = 1),
    linewidth = guide_legend(order = 1),
    linetype = guide_legend(order = 2)
  ) +
  coord_cartesian(expand = 0) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)") +
  theme(
    legend.title = element_blank(),
    legend.direction = "vertical",
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.background.x = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(
    station ~ variable,
    scales = "free_x",
    switch = "x",
    labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels_stations)
  ) +
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                     breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))

p_station_change <-
  acidification_profiles_station_obs_reconstructed %>%
  filter(station == "ALOHA" | depth <= 500,
         variable %in% c("tco2", "talk", "PO4", "temp", "sal")) %>%
  filter(driver == "observed",
         DIC_variant == "tco2") %>%
  mutate(variable = factor(variable,
                           levels = c("tco2", "talk", "PO4", "temp", "sal"))) %>%
  ggplot(aes(delta_interval,
             depth)) +
  geom_ribbon(
    aes(
      xmin = delta_interval - std.error,
      xmax = delta_interval + std.error,
      fill = variable
    ),
    alpha = 0.3
  ) +
  geom_path(aes(col = variable)) +
  scale_color_brewer(palette = "Dark2") +
  scale_fill_brewer(palette = "Dark2") +
  coord_cartesian(expand = 0) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)") +
  theme_bw() +
  theme(
    legend.position = "none",
    panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.background.x = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(
    station ~ variable,
    scales = "free_x",
    switch = "x",
    labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels_stations)
  ) +
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                     breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))

p_station_absolute <-
TS_product_mean %>%
  select(station, depth_int, tco2, talk, PO4, temp, sal) %>%
  rename(depth = depth_int) %>%
  pivot_longer(-c(station, depth),
               names_to = "variable") %>% 
  group_by(station, depth, variable) %>%
  summarise(sd = sd(value, na.rm = TRUE),
            mean = mean(value, na.rm = TRUE)) %>%
  ungroup() %>% 
  filter(station == "ALOHA" | depth <= 500,
         depth <= 3000) %>%
  mutate(variable = factor(variable,
                           levels = c("tco2", "talk", "PO4", "temp", "sal"))) %>%
  ggplot(aes(mean,
             depth)) +
  geom_ribbon(
    aes(
      xmin = mean - sd,
      xmax = mean + sd,
      fill = variable
    ),
    alpha = 0.3
  ) +
  geom_path(aes(col = variable)) +
  scale_color_brewer(palette = "Dark2") +
  scale_fill_brewer(palette = "Dark2") +
  coord_cartesian(expand = 0) +
  labs(y = "Depth (m)") +
  theme_bw() +
  theme(
    legend.position = "none",
    panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
    axis.title.x = element_blank(),
    strip.background.x = element_blank(),
    strip.placement = "outside",
    strip.text.x = element_markdown()
  ) +
  facet_grid(
    station ~ variable,
    scales = "free_x",
    switch = "x",
    labeller = labeller(variable = x_axis_labels_stations_absolute)
  ) +
  scale_y_continuous(trans = trans_reverser("sqrt"),
                     breaks = c(0, 100, 500, seq(1500, 5000, 1000)))


cowplot::plot_grid(p_station_change,
                   p_station_absolute,
                   ncol = 1,
                   align = "h")

  dpi = 600,
  bg = "white"
)
